tire `load()` function fails and goes to the catch block which just `console.error(e)`. Then `releases` stays as `[]` and README stays as `\'\'`. So if rate-limited, both would be empty!\n\nBut the issue says "很多项目" have this, suggesting it\'s not rate-limiting per se.\n\n3. **The `filterInstallAssets` is too aggressive** — hmm but we showed it\'s only filtering signature files.\n\nActually, wait. Let me re-read `filterInstallAssets`:\n```js\nexport function filterInstallAssets(assets: GitHubRelease[\'assets\']) {\n  const sigExts = [\'.asc\', \'.sig\', \'.sha256\', \'.sha512\', \'.md5\', \'.txt\']\n  return assets.filter((a) => {\n    const lower = a.name.toLowerCase()\n    return !sigExts.some((ext) => lower.endsWith(ext))\n  })\n}\n```\n\nWhat about files like:\n- `RELEASES.md` → doesn\'t match (ends with .md)\n- `checksums.txt` → filtered OUT ✓ (this is intentional)\n- `v1.0.0.sha256` → filtered OUT ✓\n\nBut what about `.json` files? Every release shows "该版本暂无安装包"\n\nIf it\'s #1, the fetchReleases is failing or returning empty.\nIf it\'s #2, filterInstallAssets is removing everything.\n\nGiven that the user says "很多项目" — I think case #1 is more likely (the releases API call is failing silently).\n\n**The fix I think is needed:**\n\n1. Add error handling for `fetchReleases` in the detail page (it currently has no `.catch()`)\n2. Also fix `fetchReadme` to handle the base64 content with newlines properly\n3. Maybe improve `filterInstallAssets` to be less restrictive — don\'t filter `.json` or show all assets with appropriate icons\n\nActually, let me look at this differently. The MOST common reason for "releases show as empty on many projects" when using GitHub API:\n\n**The GitHub API rate limit!** When hitting 60 req/hour (unauthenticated), the `/releases` endpoint returns a 403. The edge function then returns `status: 403` with an error body. The `supabase.functions.invoke` would return this as an `error`. Then `fetchReleases` throws. But in `detail/[id].tsx`:\n\n```js\nconst [rels, rm] = await Promise.all([\n  fetchReleases(owner, repo, 1),\n  fetchReadme(owner, repo).catch(() => \'\'),\n]);\n```\n\nIf `fetchReleases` throws (due to 403), the `Promise.all` rejects, and the outer `try/catch` catches it → `console.error(e)` → releases stays `[]`, readme stays `\'\'`.\n\nSo the symptom is: both releases AND readme are empty. The user sees "暂无安装包" and "暂无 README 文档" for projects that clearly have them.\n\n**Fix plan:**\n\n1. **Add `.catch()` to `fetchReleases` in detail page** — so releases and readme failures are independent, and partial data can still be shown\n2. **Fix README base64 decoding** — strip `\\n` from base64 before `atob()` call  \n3. **Improve `filterInstallAssets`** to not be too restrictive — maybe add `.json` to excluded list since json files are metadata, not installable\n4. **Consider fetching `latest release` via `/releases/latest`** endpoint instead of all releases when we just need to show the latest — but this is an optimization\n\nLet me also check if there\'s a case sensitivity issue in `filterInstallAssets`. If a file is named `app.SHA256`, the `.toLowerCase()` handles it. OK.\n\nThe primary fix: add proper error handling so releases and readme failures don\'t block each other.\n\nSecondary fix: the README base64 decode — use a more robust approach.\n\nThird consideration: many open source projects release `.tar.gz` files (Linux tarballs), which are currently passing through `filterInstallAssets` and would show up as "通用" platform. That seems correct.\n\nBut wait — could `.tar.gz` be the issue? A file ending in `.gz` doesn\'t match any of the excluded extensions, so it passes through. But does the `filterInstallAssets` accidentally exclude it? No, `.tar.gz` doesn\'t end with any of `.asc`, `.sig`, `.sha256`, `.sha512`, `.md5`, `.txt`. So it shows up. That\'s fine.\n\nOK let me focus on the actual concrete fixes:\n\n**Fix 1: Independent error handling for releases and readme in detail page**\n```js\nconst [rels, rm] = await Promise.all([\n  fetchReleases(owner, repo, 1).catch(() => []),  // Add catch\n  fetchReadme(owner, repo).catch(() => \'\'),\n]);\n```\n\n**Fix 2: Robust base64 decoding for README**\n```js\nconst rawBase64 = content.replace(/\\s/g, \'\') // strip newlines from base64\ntry {\n  // Modern approach\n  const bytes = Uint8Array.from(atob(rawBase64), c => c.charCodeAt(0))\n  return new TextDecoder().decode(bytes)\n} catch {\n  try {\n    // Legacy fallback\n    return decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(rawBase64)))\n  } catch {\n    return content // Return raw if all fails\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Fix 3: Add a state to show loading/error feedback for releases separately**\n\nThis way users understand WHY it\'s empty (API rate limit message).\n\nActually the simplest and most impactful fix is:\n1. `fetchReleases` catch → `[]` in detail page\n2. Path: [/workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/src/lib/github.ts]
Thought: 找到了两个根本原因：

1. **releases 加载失败被完全吞掉**：`Promise.all` 里 `fetchReleases` 没有 `.catch()`，一旦抛错（rate limit / 网络错误）整个 load 函数失败，releases 和 readme 全部清空
2. **README base64 解码不稳定**：`decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(content)))` 这个老套路遇到含特殊字符的 README 会 throw，fallback 返回空字符串；另外 GitHub API 返回的 base64 中含 `\n` 换行，需先清除

同时修这两处，并给 releases 加独立的错误状态提示：
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
export async function fetchReadme(owner: string, repo: string): Promise<string> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
    body: {
      action: 'readme',
      params: { owner, repo },
      token: cachedToken,
    },
  })
  if (error) {
    const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
    throw new Error(msg)
  }
  const content = data.data?.content || ''
  try {
    return decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(content)))
  } catch {
    return ''
  }
}
```
New String: ```
export async function fetchReadme(owner: string, repo: string): Promise<string> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
    body: {
      action: 'readme',
      params: { owner, repo },
      token: cachedToken,
    },
  })
  if (error) {
    const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
    throw new Error(msg)
  }
  // GitHub API 返回的 base64 中含 `\n`，必须先清除再 atob
  const raw = (data.data?.content || '').replace(/\s/g, '')
  if (!raw) return ''
  try {
    // 优先使用 TextDecoder 正确处理多字节 UTF-8 字符（中文、emoji 等）
    const bytes = Uint8Array.from(atob(raw), (c) => c.charCodeAt(0))
    return new TextDecoder().decode(bytes)
  } catch {
    try {
      // 降级方案：旧浏览器 / 纯 ASCII README
      return decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(raw)))
    } catch {
      return ''
    }
  }
}
```

Thought: 原因很清楚：`TextInput` 没有固定高度，聚焦时 Web 浏览器会给 `<input>` 添加默认 `outline`/`border` 导致高度撑大。已设了 `outlineWidth: 0` 但没有固定行高和高度。修复方法：给包裹 View 加固定高度，并给 TextInput 加 `lineHeight` 锁住行高：

```
            <View style={{
              flex: 1,
              flexDirection: 'row',
              alignItems: 'center',
              backgroundColor: '#FFFFFF',
              borderRadius: 12,
```

```
              // 用固定高度代替 paddingVertical，防止 Web 聚焦时 outline/border 撑高搜索框

                  fontSize: 15,

                  color: '#1A1A1A',
```

[Read from /workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/src/lib/downloadManager.ts is successful.]
Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-cblk1rqa5fk1/src/lib/downloadManager.ts:
     1 /**
     2  * 下载管理引擎
     3  * - 支持最多 3 个并发下载
     4  * - 每个任务可暂停 / 恢复 / 取消
     5  * - 实时回调：进度、速度（bytes/s）、完成、失败
     6  */
     7 import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system/legacy';
     8 
     9 export type DownloadStatus =
    10   | 'pending'      // 排队等待
    11   | 'downloading'  // 下载中
    12   | 'paused'       // 已暂停
    13   | 'completed'    // 完成
    14   | 'failed'       // 失败
    15   | 'cancelled';   // 已取消
    16 
    17 export interface DownloadTask {
    18   id: string;
    19   url: string;
    20   filename: string;
    21   appId: number;
    22   appName: string;
    23   owner: string;
    24   repo: string;
    25   avatarUrl: string;
    26   version: string;
    27   status: DownloadStatus;
    28   progress: number;       // 0 ~ 1
    29   bytesWritten: number;
    30   totalBytes: number;
    31   speed: number;          // bytes/s
    32   localUri: string | null;
    33   error: string | null;
    34   createdAt: number;
    35 }
    36 
    37 type ProgressCallback = (task: DownloadTask) => void;
    38 
    39 const MAX_CONCURRENT = 3;
    40 
    41 // 任务表：id -> DownloadTask
    42 const tasks = new Map<string, DownloadTask>();
    43 // DownloadResumable 实例表：id -> instance
    44 const resumables = new Map<string, FileSystem.DownloadResumable>();
    45 // 暂停快照：id -> resumeData（Base64），用于真正从断点续传
    46 const resumeSnapshots = new Map<string, string>();
    47 // 上一次收到进度回调的时间戳（用于计算速度）
    48 const lastProgressTime = new Map<string, { ts: number; bytes: number }>();
    49 // 全局订阅者
    50 const subscribers = new Set<ProgressCallback>();
    51 
    52 // 生成唯一 ID
    53 function genId(): string {
    54   return `dl_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7)}`;
    55 }
    56 
    57 // 通知所有订阅者
    58 function notify(task: DownloadTask) {
    59   subscribers.forEach((cb) => cb({ ...task }));
    60 }
    61 
    62 // 从等待队列中取下一个并发槽
    63 function flushQueue() {
    64   const downloading = [...tasks.values()].filter((t) => t.status === 'downloading').length;
    65   if (downloading >= MAX_CONCURRENT) return;
    66 
    67   const next = [...tasks.values()].find((t) => t.status === 'pending');
    68   if (next) startTask(next.id);
    69 }
    70 
    71 // 启动单个任务
    72 async function startTask(id: string) {
    73   const task = tasks.get(id);
    74   if (!task) return;
    75 
    76   task.status = 'downloading';
    77   notify(task);
    78 
    79   const localUri = FileSystem.documentDirectory + task.filename;
    80   task.localUri = localUri;
    81   lastProgressTime.set(id, { ts: Date.now(), bytes: 0 });
    82 
    83   const resumable = FileSystem.createDownloadResumable(
    84     task.url,
    85     localUri,
    86     {},
    87     (dp: FileSystem.DownloadProgressData) => {
    88       const t = tasks.get(id);
    89       if (!t || t.status !== 'downloading') return;
    90 
    91       const { totalBytesWritten, totalBytesExpectedToWrite } = dp;
    92       const prev = lastProgressTime.get(id) ?? { ts: Date.now(), bytes: 0 };
    93       const now = Date.now();
    94       const elapsed = (now - prev.ts) / 1000; // 秒
    95       const delta = totalBytesWritten - prev.bytes;
    96       const speed = elapsed > 0 ? Math.round(delta / elapsed) : 0;
    97 
    98       lastProgressTime.set(id, { ts: now, bytes: totalBytesWritten });
    99 
   100       t.bytesWritten = totalBytesWritten;
   101       t.totalBytes = totalBytesExpectedToWrite;
   102       t.progress = totalBytesExpectedToWrite > 0
   103         ? totalBytesWritten / totalBytesExpectedToWrite
   104         : 0;
   105       t.speed = speed;
   106 
   107       notify(t);
   108     }
   109   );
   110 
   111   resumables.set(id, resumable);
   112 
   113   try {
   114     const result = await resumable.downloadAsync();
   115     const t = tasks.get(id);
   116     if (!t) return;
   117 
   118     if (result) {
   119       t.status = 'completed';
   120       t.progress = 1;
   121       t.localUri = result.uri;
   122       t.speed = 0;
   123     } else {
   124       // 已被取消
   125       if (t.status !== 'cancelled') {
   126         t.status = 'cancelled';
   127       }
   128     }
   129     notify(t);
   130   } catch (e: any) {
   131     const t = tasks.get(id);
   132     if (!t) return;
   133     if (t.status !== 'cancelled' && t.status !== 'paused') {
   134       t.status = 'failed';
   135       t.error = e?.message ?? '下载失败';
   136       notify(t);
   137     }
   138   } finally {
   139     resumables.delete(id);
   140     lastProgressTime.delete(id);
   141     flushQueue();
   142   }
   143 }
   144 
   145 // ─── 公开 API ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   146 
   147 /** 订阅任意任务变更 */
   148 export function subscribe(cb: ProgressCallback): () => void {
   149   subscribers.add(cb);
   150   return () => subscribers.delete(cb);
   151 }
   152 
   153 /** 获取所有任务快照 */
   154 export function getAllTasks(): DownloadTask[] {
   155   return [...tasks.values()].sort((a, b) => b.createdAt - a.createdAt);
   156 }
   157 
   158 /** 获取单个任务 */
   159 export function getTask(id: string): DownloadTask | undefined {
   160   return tasks.get(id);
   161 }
   162 
   163 /** 查找同一 URL 的任务（避免重复下载） */
   164 export function findTaskByUrl(url: string): DownloadTask | undefined {
   165   return [...tasks.values()].find((t) => t.url === url);
   166 }
   167 
   168 /** 添加下载任务（返回任务 ID）*/
   169 export function enqueue(params: {
   170   url: string;
   171   filename: string;
   172   appId: number;
   173   appName: string;
   174   owner: string;
   175   repo: string;
   176   avatarUrl: string;
   177   version: string;
   178 }): string {
   179   const id = genId();
   180   const task: DownloadTask = {
   181     id,
   182     url: params.url,
   183     filename: params.filename,
   184     appId: params.appId,
   185     appName: params.appName,
   186     owner: params.owner,
   187     repo: params.repo,
   188     avatarUrl: params.avatarUrl,
   189     version: params.version,
   190     status: 'pending',
   191     progress: 0,
   192     bytesWritten: 0,
   193     totalBytes: 0,
   194     speed: 0,
   195     localUri: null,
   196     error: null,
   197     createdAt: Date.now(),
   198   };
   199   tasks.set(id, task);
   200   notify(task);
   201   flushQueue();
   202   return id;
   203 }
   204 
   205 /**
   206  * 重试失败/取消的任务：先清除旧记录再重新入队。
   207  * 不能直接 enqueue，因为旧 failed 任务还在 map 里，findByUrl 会返回旧任务导致 UI 不刷新。
   208  */
   209 export function retry(oldId: string): string {
   210   const old = tasks.get(oldId);
   211   if (!old) return '';
   212   // 先清除旧任务记录
   213   tasks.delete(oldId);
   214   lastProgressTime.delete(oldId);
   215   resumeSnapshots.delete(oldId);
   216   // 用相同参数重新入队
   217   return enqueue({
   218     url: old.url,
   219     filename: old.filename,
   220     appId: old.appId,
   221     appName: old.appName,
   222     owner: old.owner,
   223     repo: old.repo,
   224     avatarUrl: old.avatarUrl,
   225     version: old.version,
   226   });
   227 }
   228 
   229 /** 暂停下载，保存 resumeData 快照供后续断点续传 */
   230 export async function pause(id: string): Promise<void> {
   231   const task = tasks.get(id);
   232   if (!task || task.status !== 'downloading') return;
   233 
   234   const resumable = resumables.get(id);
   235   if (resumable) {
   236     try {
   237       const snapshot = await resumable.pauseAsync();
   238       // 保存断点快照，resume() 时使用，否则会从 0 字节重下
   239       if (snapshot?.resumeData) {
   240         resumeSnapshots.set(id, snapshot.resumeData);
   241       }
   242     } catch {
   243       // ignore
   244     }
   245     resumables.delete(id);
   246   }
   247   task.status = 'paused';
   248   task.speed = 0;
   249   notify(task);
   250 }
   251 
   252 /** 恢复下载，优先使用断点快照实现真正的断点续传 */
   253 export async function resume(id: string): Promise<void> {
   254   const task = tasks.get(id);
   255   if (!task || task.status !== 'paused') return;
   256 
   257   // 检查并发槽
   258   const downloading = [...tasks.values()].filter((t) => t.status === 'downloading').length;
   259   if (downloading >= MAX_CONCURRENT) {
   260     // 放回等待队列
   261     task.status = 'pending';
   262     notify(task);
   263     return;
   264   }
   265 
   266   task.status = 'downloading';
   267   notify(task);
   268 
   269   const localUri = task.localUri ?? FileSystem.documentDirectory + task.filename;
   270   task.localUri = localUri;
   271   lastProgressTime.set(id, { ts: Date.now(), bytes: task.bytesWritten });
   272 
   273   const progressCallback = (dp: FileSystem.DownloadProgressData) => {
   274     const t = tasks.get(id);
   275     if (!t || t.status !== 'downloading') return;
   276 
   277     const { totalBytesWritten, totalBytesExpectedToWrite } = dp;
   278     const prev = lastProgressTime.get(id) ?? { ts: Date.now(), bytes: 0 };
   279     const now = Date.now();
   280     const elapsed = (now - prev.ts) / 1000;
   281     const delta = totalBytesWritten - prev.bytes;
   282     const speed = elapsed > 0 ? Math.round(delta / elapsed) : 0;
   283 
   284     lastProgressTime.set(id, { ts: now, bytes: totalBytesWritten });
   285 
   286     t.bytesWritten = totalBytesWritten;
   287     t.totalBytes = totalBytesExpectedToWrite;
   288     t.progress = totalBytesExpectedToWrite > 0
   289       ? totalBytesWritten / totalBytesExpectedToWrite
   290       : 0;
   291     t.speed = speed;
   292     notify(t);
   293   };
   294 
   295   // 优先使用已保存的断点快照（真正的断点续传），否则回退到从头下载
   296   const savedResumeData = resumeSnapshots.get(id);
   297   resumeSnapshots.delete(id);
   298 
   299   const resumable = savedResumeData
   300     ? new FileSystem.DownloadResumable(task.url, localUri, {}, progressCallback, savedResumeData)
   301     : FileSystem.createDownloadResumable(task.url, localUri, {}, progressCallback);
   302 
   303   resumables.set(id, resumable);
   304 
   305   try {
   306     const result = await resumable.downloadAsync();
   307     const t = tasks.get(id);
   308     if (!t) return;
   309     if (result) {
   310       t.status = 'completed';
   311       t.progress = 1;
   312       t.localUri = result.uri;
   313       t.speed = 0;
   314     } else if (t.status !== 'cancelled') {
   315       t.status = 'cancelled';
   316     }
   317     notify(t);
   318   } catch (e: any) {
   319     const t = tasks.get(id);
   320     if (!t) return;
   321     if (t.status !== 'cancelled' && t.status !== 'paused') {
   322       t.status = 'failed';
   323       t.error = e?.message ?? '下载失败';
   324       notify(t);
   325     }
   326   } finally {
   327     resumables.delete(id);
   328     lastProgressTime.delete(id);
   329     flushQueue();
   330   }
   331 }
   332 
   333 /** 取消并删除任务 */
   334 export async function cancel(id: string): Promise<void> {
   335   const task = tasks.get(id);
   336   if (!task) return;
   337 
   338   const resumable = resumables.get(id);
   339   if (resumable) {
   340     try {
   341       await resumable.cancelAsync();
   342     } catch {
   343       // ignore
   344     }
   345     resumables.delete(id);
   346   }
   347 
   348   // 删除未完成的本地文件
   349   if (task.localUri && task.status !== 'completed') {
   350     try {
   351       await FileSystem.deleteAsync(task.localUri, { idempotent: true });
   352     } catch {
   353       // ignore
   354     }
   355   }
   356 
   357   tasks.delete(id);
   358   lastProgressTime.delete(id);
   359   resumeSnapshots.delete(id);
   360   flushQueue();
   361 }
   362 
   363 /** 删除已完成任务的本地文件，并从列表移除该条记录 */
   364 export async function deleteFile(id: string): Promise<void> {
   365   const task = tasks.get(id);
   366   if (!task) return;
   367 
   368   if (task.localUri) {
   369     try {
   370       await FileSystem.deleteAsync(task.localUri, { idempotent: true });
   371     } catch {
   372       // ignore
   373     }
   374   }
   375 
   376   tasks.delete(id);
   377   lastProgressTime.delete(id);
   378   // 通知订阅者刷新列表
   379   subscribers.forEach((cb) => cb({ id: '__refresh__' } as any));
   380 }
   381 
   382 /** 清空所有已完成 / 失败 / 取消的任务 */
   383 export function clearFinished(): void {
   384   for (const [id, task] of tasks.entries()) {
   385     if (['completed', 'failed', 'cancelled'].includes(task.status)) {
   386       tasks.delete(id);
   387     }
   388   }
   389   // 通知一次空变更让 UI 刷新
   390   subscribers.forEach((cb) => cb({ id: '__refresh__' } as any));
   391 }
   392 
   393 /** 格式化速度显示 */
   394 export function formatSpeed(bytesPerSec: number): string {
   395   if (bytesPerSec <= 0) return '';
   396   if (bytesPerSec < 1024) return `${bytesPerSec} B/s`;
   397   if (bytesPerSec < 1024 * 1024) return `${(bytesPerSec / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB/s`;
   398   return `${(bytesPerSec / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)} MB/s`;
   399 }
   400 
   401 /** 格式化文件大小 */
   402 export function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
   403   if (!bytes || bytes <= 0) return '';
   404   if (bytes < 1024) return `${bytes} B`;
   405   if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return `${(bytes / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB`;
   406   return `${(bytes / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1)} MB`;
   407 }

Delete temp file\n\nThis adds complexity but is the correct approach for public Downloads access.\n\nLet me implement this properly in `downloadManager.ts`:\n- `startTask` downloads to temp `documentDirectory/temp_<id>/filename`\n- On completion, calls `moveToDownloads(localUri, filename)` which uses SAF to copy to Downloads/开源应用商店/\n- The final `localUri` is updated to the SAF content URI or stays as temp if SAF unavailable\n\nFor iOS: `documentDirectory` is fine (Files app can access it), no Downloads folder concept.\nFor Web: `documentDirectory` or nothing (browser handles downloads differently).\n\nLet me write this implementation now. Platform check\n\nActually, for simplicity and to avoid requiring user interaction for directory selection, let me use a different approach:\n\n**ANDROID: Use the app\'s external files directory**\n\n`FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework` aside, on Android there\'s also `FileSystem.documentDirectory` which on Android maps to internal storage. But `FileSystem.cacheDirectory` maps to the cache dir.\n\nActually, I just realized: in `expo-file-system`, `documentDirectory` on Android IS the app\'s internal files directory. \'\') + APP_DIR_NAME + \'/\'\n  \n  if (Platform.OS !== \'android\') {\n    await FileSystem.makeDirectoryAsync(fallback, { intermediates: true }).catch(() => null)\n    return fallback\n  }\n  \n  // Use cached value\n  if (_safDirUri) return _safDirUri\n  \n  // Check AsyncStorage\n  const stored = await AsyncStorage.getItem(SAF_DIR_KEY).catch(() => null)\n  if (stored) {\n    try {\n      await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.readDirectoryAsync(stored)\n      _safDirUri = stored\n      return stored\n    } catch {\n      // Permission revoked\n      _safDirUri = null\n      await AsyncStorage.removeItem(SAF_DIR_KEY).catch(() => null)\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Request SAF permission\n  const result = await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.requestDirectoryPermissionsAsync()\n  if (!result.granted) {\n    await FileSystem.makeDirectoryAsync(fallback, { intermediates: true }).catch(() => null)\n    return fallback\n  }\n  \n  // Create 开源应用商店 subdirectory\n  let dirUri = result.directoryUri\n  try {\n    dirUri = await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.makeDirectoryAsync(dirUri, APP_DIR_NAME)\n  } catch {\n    // Directory might already exist, try to find it\n    const entries = await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.readDirectoryAsync(dirUri).catch(() => [])\n    // If we can\'t create subdirectory, use the parent\n  }\n  \n  _safDirUri = dirUri\n  await AsyncStorage.setItem(SAF_DIR_KEY, dirUri).catch(() => null)\n  return dirUri\n}\n```\n\nActually, `StorageAccessFramework.makeDirectoryAsync` - I\'m still not sure this exists in expo-file-system/legacy.      4  * - APK 文件：完成后显示「安装」，调起 Android 系统包安装器

    35 /** 判断文件是否为 APK 安装包 */
    36 function isApkFile(filename: string): boolean {
    37   return filename.toLowerCase().endsWith('.apk');
    38 }

    40 /** 根据文件名推断 MIME 类型，用于 expo-sharing */
    41 function getMimeType(filename: string): string {
    42   const lower = filename.toLowerCase();
    43   if (lower.endsWith('.apk')) return 'application/vnd.android.package-archive';
    44   if (lower.endsWith('.zip')) return 'application/zip';
    45   if (lower.endsWith('.tar.gz') || lower.endsWith('.tgz')) return 'application/gzip';
    46   if (lower.endsWith('.deb')) return 'application/vnd.debian.binary-package';
    47   if (lower.endsWith('.rpm')) return 'application/x-rpm';
    48   if (lower.endsWith('.dmg') || lower.endsWith('.pkg')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    49   if (lower.endsWith('.exe') || lower.endsWith('.msi')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    50   if (lower.endsWith('.appimage')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    51   if (lower.endsWith('.ipa')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    52   return 'application/octet-stream';
    53 }
    54 
    55 /** 打开已下载的文件：APK 触发安装，其他文件调起系统「打开方式」 */
    56 async function openLocalFile(localUri: string, filename: string) {
    57   // Web 平台：无本地文件，无法 sharing
    58   if (Platform.OS === 'web') return;
    59   try {
    60     const mimeType = getMimeType(filename);
    61     const available = await Sharing.isAvailableAsync();
    62     if (available) {
    63       await Sharing.shareAsync(localUri, { mimeType, dialogTitle: '打开文件' });
    64     }
    65   } catch (e) {
    66     console.warn('openLocalFile error:', e);
    67   }
    68 }

    70 export default function DownloadProgressButton({
    71   downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version,
    72   compact = false,
    73 }: Props) {
    74   const { enqueue, retry, pause, resume, cancel, findByUrl } = useDownload();
    75   const task: DownloadTask | undefined = findByUrl(downloadUrl);
    76   const status = task?.status;
    77   const isApk = isApkFile(filename);
    78 
    79   const handlePress = () => {
    80     if (!task || status === 'cancelled') {
    81       // 全新下载
    82       enqueue({ url: downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version });
    83       return;
    84     }
    85     if (status === 'failed') {
    86       // 重试：通过 retry(id) 先删除旧任务再重新入队，避免 findByUrl 返回旧失败任务
    87       retry(task.id);
    88       return;
    89     }
    90     if (status === 'completed') {
    91       // 打开文件：APK→安装，其他→系统打开方式
    92       if (task.localUri) openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);
    93       return;
    94     }
    95     if (status === 'downloading') { pause(task.id); return; }
    96     if (status === 'paused') { resume(task.id); return; }
    97     if (status === 'pending') { cancel(task.id); return; }
    98   };
    99 
   100   // ── 已完成 ──────────────────────────────────────────
   101   if (status === 'completed') {
   102     return (
   103       <Pressable
   104         onPress={handlePress}
   105         style={{
   106           paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
   107           paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
   108           borderRadius: 24,
   109           backgroundColor: GREEN,
   110         }}
   111       >
   112         <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FFFFFF' }}>
   113           {isApk ? '安装' : '打开'}
   114         </Text>
   115       </Pressable>
   116     );
   117   }
   118 
   119   // ── 下载中 / 暂停 / 排队 ──────────────────────────
   120   if (task && (status === 'downloading' || status === 'paused' || status === 'pending')) {
   121     const progress = task.progress;
   122     const strokeDashoffset = CIRCUMFERENCE * (1 - progress);
   123     const isPaused = status === 'paused';
   124     const isPending = status === 'pending';
   125     const accentColor = isPaused ? ORANGE : BLUE;
   126 
   127     if (compact) {
   128       return (
   129         <Pressable onPress={handlePress} style={{ alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', width: 48, height: 32 }}>
   130           <Svg width={28} height={28} viewBox="0 0 28 28">
   131             <Circle cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS} stroke="#E0E0E0" strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none" />
   132             {!isPending && (
   133               <Circle
   134                 cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS}
   135                 stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none"
   136                 strokeDasharray={`${CIRCUMFERENCE} ${CIRCUMFERENCE}`}
   137                 strokeDashoffset={strokeDashoffset}
   138                 strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="14,14"
   139               />
   140             )}
   141           </Svg>
   142           <View style={{ position: 'absolute' }}>
   143             <Ionicons
   144               name={isPending ? 'hourglass-outline' : isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'}
   145               size={11} color={accentColor}
   146             />
   147           </View>
   148         </Pressable>
   149       );
   150     }
   151 
   152     const percent = Math.round(progress * 100);
   153     const speedStr = formatSpeed(task.speed);
   154     return (
   155       <Pressable onPress={handlePress} style={{ alignItems: 'center', gap: 4, minWidth: 60 }}>
   156         <View style={{ position: 'relative', width: 44, height: 44 }}>
   157           <Svg width={44} height={44} viewBox="0 0 44 44">
   158             <Circle cx={22} cy={22} r={18} stroke="#E5E5E5" strokeWidth={3} fill="none" />
   159             {!isPending && (
   160               <Circle
   161                 cx={22} cy={22} r={18}
   162                 stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={3} fill="none"
   163                 strokeDasharray={`${2 * Math.PI * 18} ${2 * Math.PI * 18}`}
   164                 strokeDashoffset={(2 * Math.PI * 18) * (1 - progress)}
   165                 strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="22,22"
   166               />
   167             )}
   168           </Svg>
   169           <View style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0, alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
   170             {isPending
   171               ? <Ionicons name="hourglass-outline" size={16} color="#AAAAAA" />
   172               : <Ionicons name={isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'} size={15} color={accentColor} />}
   173           </View>
   174         </View>
   175         <Text style={{ fontSize: 11, color: accentColor, fontWeight: '600' }}>
   176           {isPending ? '等待中' : isPaused ? `${percent}% 已暂停` : `${percent}%`}
   177         </Text>
   178         {speedStr && !isPaused ? <Text style={{ fontSize: 10, color: '#999999' }}>{speedStr}</Text> : null}
   179       </Pressable>
   180     );
   181   }
   182 
   183   // ── 失败 ────────────────────────────────────────────
   184   if (status === 'failed') {
   185     return (
   186       <Pressable
   187         onPress={handlePress}
   188         style={{

   196           重试
   197         </Text>
   198       </Pressable>
   199     );
   200   }
   201 
   202   // ── 初始状态 ─────────────────────────────────────────
   203   return (
   204     <Pressable

     1 /**
     2  * 全局下载状态 Context
     3  * 订阅 downloadManager 的所有任务变更，统一向组件树分发
     4  */
     5 import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
     6 import * as DM from '@/lib/downloadManager';
     7 import type { DownloadTask } from '@/lib/downloadManager';
     8 
     9 interface DownloadContextValue {
    10   tasks: DownloadTask[];
    11   enqueue: (params: Parameters<typeof DM.enqueue>[0]) => string;
    12   retry: (oldId: string) => string;
    13   pause: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
    14   resume: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
    15   cancel: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
    16   deleteFile: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
    17   clearFinished: () => void;
    18   findByUrl: (url: string) => DownloadTask | undefined;
    19   activeCount: number;
    20 }
    21 
    22 const DownloadContext = createContext<DownloadContextValue | null>(null);
    23 
    24 export function DownloadProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
    25   const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<DownloadTask[]>(() => DM.getAllTasks());
    26   // 防抖合并 notify，每 200ms 刷新一次防止高频重渲染
    27   const pendingRef = useRef(false);
    28 
    29   useEffect(() => {
    30     const unsubscribe = DM.subscribe(() => {
    31       if (pendingRef.current) return;
    32       pendingRef.current = true;
    33       setTimeout(() => {
    34         setTasks(DM.getAllTasks());
    35         pendingRef.current = false;
    36       }, 150);
    37     });
    38     return unsubscribe;
    39   }, []);
    40 
    41   const activeCount = tasks.filter(
    42     (t) => t.status === 'pending' || t.status === 'downloading'
    43   ).length;
    44 
    45   const value: DownloadContextValue = {
    46     tasks,
    47     enqueue: DM.enqueue,
    48     retry: (oldId) => {
    49       const newId = DM.retry(oldId);
    50       setTasks(DM.getAllTasks());
    51       return newId;
    52     },
    53     pause: DM.pause,
    54     resume: DM.resume,
    55     cancel: DM.cancel,
    56     deleteFile: DM.deleteFile,
    57     clearFinished: () => {
    58       DM.clearFinished();
    59       setTasks(DM.getAllTasks());
    60     },
    61     findByUrl: DM.findTaskByUrl,
    62     activeCount,
    63   };
    64 
    65   return (
    66     <DownloadContext.Provider value={value}>
    67       {children}
    68     </DownloadContext.Provider>
    69   );
    70 }
    71 
    72 export function useDownload(): DownloadContextValue {
    73   const ctx = useContext(DownloadContext);
    74   if (!ctx) throw new Error('useDownload must be used inside <DownloadProvider>');
    75   return ctx;
    76 }

Let me design the implementation:\n\nThe key challenge:\n1. `expo-file-system/legacy`\'s `StorageAccessFramework` requires user to pick a directory via system picker\n2. We want to default to Downloads/开源应用商店/ \n3. We need to create the subdirectory\n\nThe approach I\'ll take:\n1. In `downloadManager.ts`:\n   - Add `initDownloadDir()` that on Android uses SAF to get/request Downloads directory access\n   - Create `开源应用商店` subfolder inside it\n   - Cache the directory URI\n   - Download files to this SAF directory (or temp + copy)\n\n2. The problem with downloading to SAF directly: `createDownloadResumable` needs a `file://` URI, not a SAF `content://` URI\n   - So: download to temp `documentDirectory/dl_temp_<id>/filename`\n   - After completion: copy to SAF Downloads/开源应用商店/ using `FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.copyAsync`\n   - Delete temp file\n   - Update `task.localUri` to the SAF content URI\n\n3. Let me check the actual API.\n\nFrom expo-file-system docs:\n```\nFileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.copyAsync(options: CopyOptions): Promise<void>\n  - from: URI string\n  - to: URI string\n```\n\nIt returns `Promise<void>`. But we need the destination URI. That\'s the problem - we don\'t know the destination URI after copying.\n\nAlternative: Use `FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.createFileAsync(dirUri, filename, mimeType)` which RETURNS the file URI, then copy using regular `FileSystem.copyAsync({ from: tempUri, to: safFileUri })`.\n\n`FileSystem.copyAsync({ from, to })` - this copies from `from` to `to`. If `to` is a `content://` URI (SAF), it might work on Android using ContentResolver.\n\nActually wait - regular `FileSystem.copyAsync` might not support SAF `content://` URIs as destination. Let me think...\n\nFrom Expo source code analysis, `FileSystem.copyAsync` on Android handles `file://` URIs. For `content://` URIs, you need to use `StorageAccessFramework` methods.\n\nSo the correct approach:\n1. Create file: `const destUri = await StorageAccessFramework.createFileAsync(dirUri, filename, mimeType)` → returns content:// URI\n2. Write content: `await StorageAccessFramework.writeAsStringAsync(destUri, base64Content, { encoding: \'base64\' })` → memory intensive\n\nOR:\n2. Use `StorageAccessFramework.copyAsync({ from: tempFileUri, to: destUri })` where destUri is the content:// file URI\n\nLet me check if `StorageAccessFramework.copyAsync({ from: \'file://...\', to: \'content://...\' })` works. Based on Expo\'s Android implementation, `copyAsync` calls `MediaStore` or `FileUtils.copy` which should handle cross-type URIs.\n\nI\'ll go with this approach and see. If `copyAsync` doesn\'t work for cross-URI-type copying, the `writeAsStringAsync` approach would be the fallback.\n\nActually, you know what, I think the best approach that\'s DEFINITELY going to work is:\n\n1. Download to temp: `documentDirectory + \'temp_\' + id + \'_\' + filename`\n2. After completion, try SAF copy:\n   - Request SAF Downloads permission (once, stored in AsyncStorage)\n   - `createFileAsync` to create file in Downloads/开源应用商店/\n   - `writeAsStringAsync` with base64 content (yes, this is memory-intensive but for APK-size files on modern Android devices, it should work for files up to ~50MB)\n   - Delete temp file\n   - Update localUri to SAF URI\n3. For files > 50MB, keep temp file in documentDirectory and show a note\n\nActually for the initial implementation, let me just use `StorageAccessFramework.copyAsync` and hope it works for file:// → content:// copying. If not, we can fallback.\n\nAlternatively, a much simpler approach: instead of copying after download, I can modify `startTask` to:\n1. Get the SAF directory URI\n2. Pre-create the destination file: `safFileUri = createFileAsync(dirUri, filename, mimeType)`  \n3. Download to temp: `downloadAsync` to documentDirectory\n4. Copy from temp to safFileUri using `copyAsync`\n5. Clean up temp\n\nThis has the issue that `createDownloadResumable` only writes to file:// URIs. But we can work around it.\n\nLet me just write the implementation with best-effort SAF support:\n\n```typescript\nimport { Platform } from \'react-native\'\nimport AsyncStorage from \'@react-native-async-storage/async-storage\'\n\nconst APP_FOLDER_NAME = \'开源应用商店\'\nconst SAF_URI_STORAGE_KEY = \'@openappstore/saf_downloads_uri\'\n\n// 内存缓存，避免每次下载都读 AsyncStorage\nlet _safDirUri: string | null | undefined = undefined // undefined = not initialized yet\n\nasync function getSafDirUri(): Promise<string | null> {\n  if (_safDirUri !== undefined) return _safDirUri\n  const stored = await AsyncStorage.getItem(SAF_URI_STORAGE_KEY).catch(() => null)\n  if (stored) {\n    // 验证权限是否仍有效\n    try {\n      await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.readDirectoryAsync(stored)\n /**
```
 * 下载管理引擎
 * - 支持最多 3 个并发下载
 * - 每个任务可暂停 / 恢复 / 取消
 * - 实时回调：进度、速度（bytes/s）、完成、失败
```

New String: ```
/**
 * 下载管理引擎
 * - 支持最多 3 个并发下载
 * - 每个任务可暂停 / 恢复 / 取消
 * - 实时回调：进度、速度（bytes/s）、完成、失败
 * - Android：下载完成后自动将文件移至 Downloads/开源应用商店/ 公共目录（SAF）
 */
import { Platform } from 'react-native';
import AsyncStorage from '@react-native-async-storage/async-storage';
import * as FileSystem from 'expo-file-system/legacy';

const APP_FOLDER_NAME = '开源应用商店';
const SAF_URI_KEY = '@openappstore/saf_downloads_uri';

// 内存缓存 SAF 目录 URI；undefined = 尚未初始化，null = 无权限/非 Android
let _safDirUri: string | null | undefined = undefined;

/** 从 AsyncStorage 恢复上次已授权的 SAF 目录 URI，并验证权限是否仍有效 */
async function loadSafUri(): Promise<string | null> {
  if (_safDirUri !== undefined) return _safDirUri;
  const stored = await AsyncStorage.getItem(SAF_URI_KEY).catch(() => null);
  if (stored) {
    try {
      await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.readDirectoryAsync(stored);
      _safDirUri = stored;
      return stored;
    } catch {
      // 权限被吊销，清除缓存
      _safDirUri = null;
      await AsyncStorage.removeItem(SAF_URI_KEY).catch(() => null);
    }
  } else {
    _safDirUri = null;
  }
  return null;
}

/**
 * 弹出系统文件夹选择器，引导用户授权 Download 目录。
 * 授权成功后自动在其中创建「开源应用商店」子目录并持久化 URI。
 * 返回 true 表示已成功获取目录权限。
 */
export async function requestDownloadsPermission(): Promise<boolean> {
  if (Platform.OS !== 'android') return false;
  try {
    // 预设初始路径为 primary:Download，用户只需点「使用此文件夹」即可
    const result = await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.requestDirectoryPermissionsAsync(
      'content://com.android.externalstorage.documents/tree/primary%3ADownload'
    );
    if (!result.granted) return false;

    // 尝试在所选目录下创建「开源应用商店」子目录
    let finalUri = result.directoryUri;
    try {
      finalUri = await (FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework as any).makeDirectoryAsync(
        result.directoryUri,
        APP_FOLDER_NAME
      );
    } catch {
      // makeDirectoryAsync 可能不存在（老版本）或目录已存在，使用父目录
    }

    _safDirUri = finalUri;
    await AsyncStorage.setItem(SAF_URI_KEY, finalUri).catch(() => null);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/** 清除已保存的 SAF 授权（用于设置页重置） */
export async function resetDownloadsPermission(): Promise<void> {
  _safDirUri = null;
  await AsyncStorage.removeItem(SAF_URI_KEY).catch(() => null);
}

/** 检查是否已有 Downloads SAF 权限 */
export async function hasDownloadsPermission(): Promise<boolean> {
  if (Platform.OS !== 'android') return false;
  const uri = await loadSafUri();
  return uri !== null;
}

/**
 * 将已下载到 documentDirectory 的临时文件复制到 SAF Downloads 目录。
 * 成功则返回新的 content:// URI 并删除临时文件；失败则返回原 tempUri。
 */
async function moveToSafDownloads(tempUri: string, filename: string): Promise<string> {
  try {
    const dirUri = await loadSafUri();
    if (!dirUri) return tempUri;

    // 推断 MIME 类型
    const lower = filename.toLowerCase();
    let mimeType = 'application/octet-stream';
    if (lower.endsWith('.apk'))  mimeType = 'application/vnd.android.package-archive';
    else if (lower.endsWith('.zip'))  mimeType = 'application/zip';
    else if (lower.endsWith('.tar.gz') || lower.endsWith('.tgz')) mimeType = 'application/gzip';
    else if (lower.endsWith('.deb'))  mimeType = 'application/vnd.debian.binary-package';

    // 在 SAF 目录中创建目标文件（若同名文件已存在，会自动追加编号）
    const destUri = await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.createFileAsync(
      dirUri, filename, mimeType
    );

    // 将 file:// 临时文件复制到 content:// SAF 文件
    await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.copyAsync({ from: tempUri, to: destUri });

    // 删除临时文件
    await FileSystem.deleteAsync(tempUri, { idempotent: true }).catch(() => null);

    return destUri;
  } catch {
    // SAF 操作失败，保留临时文件路径
    return tempUri;
  }
}
```

   202       const prev = lastProgressTime.get(id) ?? { ts: Date.now(), bytes: 0 };
   203       const now = Date.now();
   204       const elapsed = (now - prev.ts) / 1000; // 秒
   205       const delta = totalBytesWritten - prev.bytes;
   206       const speed = elapsed > 0 ? Math.round(delta / elapsed) : 0;

```
export function DownloadProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<DownloadTask[]>(() => DM.getAllTasks());
  // 防抖合并 notify，每 200ms 刷新一次防止高频重渲染
  const pendingRef = useRef(false);
  // 是否已请求过 SAF Downloads 权限（本次 App 生命周期内）
  const safRequestedRef = useRef(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const unsubscribe = DM.subscribe(() => {
      if (pendingRef.current) return;
      pendingRef.current = true;
      setTimeout(() => {
        setTasks(DM.getAllTasks());
        pendingRef.current = false;
      }, 150);
    });
    // App 启动时恢复已有的 SAF 权限缓存（不弹窗，只读 AsyncStorage）
    if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
      DM.hasDownloadsPermission().then((has) => { if (has) safRequestedRef.current = true; });
    }
    return unsubscribe;
  }, []);

  const activeCount = tasks.filter(
    (t) => t.status === 'pending' || t.status === 'downloading'
  ).length;

  /** 第一次在 Android 上触发下载时，自动弹出 SAF 目录授权对话框 */
  const enqueueWithSaf = (params: Parameters<typeof DM.enqueue>[0]): string => {
    if (Platform.OS === 'android' && !safRequestedRef.current) {
      safRequestedRef.current = true;
      DM.requestDownloadsPermission(); // 不 await，弹窗在后台处理
    }
    return DM.enqueue(params);
  };

  const value: DownloadContextValue = {
    tasks,
    enqueue: enqueueWithSaf,
    retry: (oldId) => {
      const newId = DM.retry(oldId);
      setTasks(DM.getAllTasks());
      return newId;
    },
    pause: DM.pause,
    resume: DM.resume,
    cancel: DM.cancel,
    deleteFile: DM.deleteFile,
    clearFinished: () => {
      DM.clearFinished();
      setTasks(DM.getAllTasks());
    },
    findByUrl: DM.findTaskByUrl,
    activeCount,
    requestDownloadsPermission: DM.requestDownloadsPermission,
  };
```

   182 async function startTask(id: string) {
   183   const task = tasks.get(id);
   184   if (!task) return;
   185 
   186   task.status = 'downloading';
   187   notify(task);
   188 
   189   // Android 下载到临时路径，完成后通过 SAF 移至 Downloads/开源应用商店/
   190   // 其他平台直接下载到 documentDirectory 的 APP 子目录
   191   const dir = (FileSystem.documentDirectory ?? '') +
   192     (Platform.OS === 'android' ? `dl_temp_${id}/` : `${APP_FOLDER_NAME}/`);
   193   await FileSystem.makeDirectoryAsync(dir, { intermediates: true }).catch(() => null);
   194   const localUri = dir + task.filename;
   195   task.localUri = localUri;
   196   lastProgressTime.set(id, { ts: Date.now(), bytes: 0 });
   197 
   198   const resumable = FileSystem.createDownloadResumable(
   199     task.url,
   200     localUri,
   201     {},
   202     (dp: FileSystem.DownloadProgressData) => {
   203       const t = tasks.get(id);
   204       if (!t || t.status !== 'downloading') return;
   205 
   206       const { totalBytesWritten, totalBytesExpectedToWrite } = dp;
   207       const prev = lastProgressTime.get(id) ?? { ts: Date.now(), bytes: 0 };
   208       const now = Date.now();
   209       const elapsed = (now - prev.ts) / 1000; // 秒
   210       const delta = totalBytesWritten - prev.bytes;
   211       const speed = elapsed > 0 ? Math.round(delta / elapsed) : 0;
   212 
   213       lastProgressTime.set(id, { ts: now, bytes: totalBytesWritten });
   214 
   215       t.bytesWritten = totalBytesWritten;
   216       t.totalBytes = totalBytesExpectedToWrite;
   217       t.progress = totalBytesExpectedToWrite > 0
   218         ? totalBytesWritten / totalBytesExpectedToWrite
   219         : 0;
   220       t.speed = speed;
   221 
   222       notify(t);
   223     }
   224   );
   225 
   226   resumables.set(id, resumable);
   227 
   228   try {
   229     const result = await resumable.downloadAsync();
   230     const t = tasks.get(id);
   231     if (!t) return;
   232 
   233     if (result) {
   234       t.status = 'completed';
   235       t.progress = 1;
   236       t.speed = 0;
   237       // Android：将临时文件移到 SAF Downloads/开源应用商店/，非 Android 直接用原路径
   238       if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
   239         t.localUri = await moveToSafDownloads(result.uri, task.filename);
   240         // 清理空的临时目录
   241         await FileSystem.deleteAsync(dir, { idempotent: true }).catch(() => null);
   242       } else {
   243         t.localUri = result.uri;
   244       }
   245     } else {
   246       // 已被取消
   247       if (t.status !== 'cancelled') {
   248         t.status = 'cancelled';
   249       }
   250     }
   251     notify(t);
   252   } catch (e: any) {
   253     const t = tasks.get(id);
   254     if (!t) return;
   255     if (t.status !== 'cancelled' && t.status !== 'paused') {
   256       t.status = 'failed';
   257       t.error = e?.message ?? '下载失败';
   258       notify(t);
   259     }
   260   } finally {
   261     resumables.delete(id);
   262     lastProgressTime.delete(id);
   263     flushQueue();
   264   }
   265 }

    55 /** 打开已下载的文件：APK 触发安装，其他文件调起系统「打开方式」 */
    56 async function openLocalFile(localUri: string, filename: string) {
    57   // Web 平台：无本地文件，无法 sharing
    58   if (Platform.OS === 'web') return;
    59   try {
    60     const mimeType = getMimeType(filename);
    61     const available = await Sharing.isAvailableAsync();
    62     if (available) {
    63       await Sharing.shareAsync(localUri, { mimeType, dialogTitle: '打开文件' });
    64     }
    65   } catch (e) {
    66     console.warn('openLocalFile error:', e);
    67   }
    68 }
    69 
    70 export default function DownloadProgressButton({
    71   downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version,
    72   compact = false,
    73 }: Props) {
    74   const { enqueue, retry, pause, resume, cancel, findByUrl } = useDownload();
    75   const task: DownloadTask | undefined = findByUrl(downloadUrl);
    76   const status = task?.status;
    77   const isApk = isApkFile(filename);
    78 
    79   const handlePress = () => {
    80     if (!task || status === 'cancelled') {
    81       // 全新下载
    82       enqueue({ url: downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version });
    83       return;
    84     }
    85     if (status === 'failed') {
    86       // 重试：通过 retry(id) 先删除旧任务再重新入队，避免 findByUrl 返回旧失败任务
    87       retry(task.id);
    88       return;
    89     }
    90     if (status === 'completed') {
    91       // 打开文件：APK→安装，其他→系统打开方式
    92       if (task.localUri) openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);
    93       return;
    94     }
    95     if (status === 'downloading') { pause(task.id); return; }
    96     if (status === 'paused') { resume(task.id); return; }
    97     if (status === 'pending') { cancel(task.id); return; }
    98   };
    99 
   100   // ── 已完成 ──────────────────────────────────────────

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe user wants: when a file is an installer (APK, IPA, EXE, DMG, DEB, etc.), automatically trigger the installer after download completes.\n\nCurrently, the download completes and shows "安装"/"打开" button that the user must press manually.\n\nThe change needed:\n1. In `downloadManager.ts`, after `t.status = \'completed\'`, if the file is an installer, emit a special event/callback OR we can add an `autoOpen` mechanism.\n\n2. Better approach: In `DownloadContext.tsx`, when a task transitions to `completed`, check if it\'s an installer file and auto-trigger the open/install function.\n\n3. Or even simpler: In `DownloadProgressButton.tsx`, use `useEffect` to watch for task status change to \'completed\' and auto-trigger `openLocalFile` if it\'s an APK.\n\nThe cleanest approach is in `DownloadContext.tsx` - subscribe to task changes and when a task transitions to `completed` AND it\'s an installer file, auto-invoke the install function.\n\nBut `DownloadContext` doesn\'t have access to the `openLocalFile` function (that\'s in the button component). \n\nBetter: put the auto-install logic in `DownloadProgressButton.tsx` since it has both the task state and the `openLocalFile` function. Use a `useEffect` that watches task status and auto-triggers when status changes to \'completed\' AND filename is an installer.\n\nThe install file types:\n- `.apk` → Android package installer\n- `.ipa` → iOS (can\'t auto-install, needs AltStore etc.)\n- `.exe`, `.msi` → Windows\n- `.dmg`, `.pkg` → macOS  \n- `.deb`, `.rpm`, `.appimage` → Linux\n\nOn Android, only `.apk` makes sense for auto-install.\nOn iOS, `.ipa` can\'t be installed from within an app without special tools.\nOn macOS/Windows/Linux (web/desktop), auto-install is generally not possible from a React Native app.\n\nSo the practical auto-install is:\n- Android: `.apk` → auto-trigger `Sharing.shareAsync` with APK MIME type (which opens system package installer)\n- Other platforms: show the button as before\n\nIn `DownloadProgressButton.tsx`:\n- Add `useEffect` that watches `task?.status`\n- When status changes to `completed` AND filename ends with `.apk` AND `Platform.OS === \'android\'`\n- Auto-call `openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename)`\n\nNeed to be careful about:\n1. Only triggering once (use a ref to track if auto-install was triggered)\n2. Only triggering for the specific button instance (not all buttons)\n3. Not triggering if the user navigated away\n\nImplementation:\n```tsx\nconst autoInstallRef = useRef(false);\n\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (\n    task?.status === \'completed\' &&\n    task.localUri &&\n    isApk &&\n    Platform.OS === \'android\' &&\n    !autoInstallRef.current\n  ) {\n    autoInstallRef.current = true;\n    openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);\n  }\n}, [task?.status, task?.localUri, isApk, filename]);\n```\n\nThis is clean, only runs when status becomes \'completed\', and the ref prevents double-triggering.\n\nThe issue: `autoInstallRef.current` starts as `false`, so every time the component mounts with a completed task (e.g., user navigates back to the page), it would auto-open again. \n\nFix: initialize the ref to `true` if the task is already completed when the component mounts:\n```tsx\nconst autoInstallRef = useRef(task?.status === \'completed\');\n```\n\nThis way:\n- If task starts as pending/downloading → ref is false → when it completes → auto-install triggers once\n- If task was already completed when component mounts → ref is true → no auto-install (user must press button)\n\nThis is the correct behavior.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)
</action>

     1 /**
     2  * 下载进度按钮
     3  * 状态：初始 → 下载中（进度圆弧 + 速度）→ 完成 → 打开/安装
     4  * - APK 文件：完成后显示「安装」，调起 Android 系统包安装器
     5  * - 其他文件：完成后显示「打开」，调起系统分享/打开方式对话框
     6  * - 重试：先清除旧失败任务再重新入队，彻底解决重试无效问题
     7  */
     8 import { View, Text, Pressable, Platform } from 'react-native';
     9 import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
    10 import Svg, { Circle } from 'react-native-svg';
    11 import { Ionicons } from '@expo/vector-icons';
    12 import * as Sharing from 'expo-sharing';
    13 import { useDownload } from '@/ctx/DownloadContext';
    14 import { formatSpeed } from '@/lib/downloadManager';
    15 import type { DownloadTask } from '@/lib/downloadManager';
    16 
    17 interface Props {
    18   downloadUrl: string;
    19   filename: string;
    20   appId: number;
    21   appName: string;
    22   owner: string;
    23   repo: string;
    24   avatarUrl: string;
    25   version: string;
    26   /** 紧凑模式：用于 AppCard 列表场景 */
    27   compact?: boolean;

    29 
    30 const BLUE = '#1677FF';
    31 const GREEN = '#52C41A';
    32 const ORANGE = '#FA8C16';
    33 const RADIUS = 11;
    34 const CIRCUMFERENCE = 2 * Math.PI * RADIUS;
    35 
    36 /** 判断文件是否为 APK 安装包 */
    37 function isApkFile(filename: string): boolean {
    38   return filename.toLowerCase().endsWith('.apk');
    39 }
    40 
    41 /** 根据文件名推断 MIME 类型，用于 expo-sharing */
    42 function getMimeType(filename: string): string {
    43   const lower = filename.toLowerCase();
    44   if (lower.endsWith('.apk')) return 'application/vnd.android.package-archive';
    45   if (lower.endsWith('.zip')) return 'application/zip';
    46   if (lower.endsWith('.tar.gz') || lower.endsWith('.tgz')) return 'application/gzip';
    47   if (lower.endsWith('.deb')) return 'application/vnd.debian.binary-package';
    48   if (lower.endsWith('.rpm')) return 'application/x-rpm';
    49   if (lower.endsWith('.dmg') || lower.endsWith('.pkg')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    50   if (lower.endsWith('.exe') || lower.endsWith('.msi')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    51   if (lower.endsWith('.appimage')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    52   if (lower.endsWith('.ipa')) return 'application/octet-stream';
    53   return 'application/octet-stream';
    54 }
    55 
    56 /** 打开已下载的文件：APK 触发安装，其他文件调起系统「打开方式」 */
    57 async function openLocalFile(localUri: string, filename: string) {
    58   // Web 平台：无本地文件，无法 sharing
    59   if (Platform.OS === 'web') return;
    60   try {
    61     const mimeType = getMimeType(filename);
    62     const available = await Sharing.isAvailableAsync();
    63     if (available) {
    64       await Sharing.shareAsync(localUri, { mimeType, dialogTitle: '打开文件' });
    65     }
    66   } catch (e) {
    67     console.warn('openLocalFile error:', e);
    68   }
    69 }
    70 
    71 export default function DownloadProgressButton({
    72   downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version,
    73   compact = false,
    74 }: Props) {
    75   const { enqueue, retry, pause, resume, cancel, findByUrl } = useDownload();
    76   const task: DownloadTask | undefined = findByUrl(downloadUrl);
    77   const status = task?.status;
    78   const isApk = isApkFile(filename);
    79 
    80   // 下载完成后自动调起安装器（仅 Android APK）
    81   // 初始值：若挂载时任务已完成则置 true，避免页面切换回来时重复弹窗
    82   const autoInstallFiredRef = useRef(task?.status === 'completed');
    83   useEffect(() => {
    84     if (
    85       status === 'completed' &&
    86       task?.localUri &&
    87       isApk &&
    88       Platform.OS === 'android' &&
    89       !autoInstallFiredRef.current
    90     ) {
    91       autoInstallFiredRef.current = true;
    92       openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);
    93     }
    94   }, [status, task?.localUri, isApk, filename]);
    95 
    96   const handlePress = () => {
    97     if (!task || status === 'cancelled') {
    98       // 全新下载
    99       enqueue({ url: downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version });
   100       return;
   101     }
   102     if (status === 'failed') {
   103       // 重试：通过 retry(id) 先删除旧任务再重新入队，避免 findByUrl 返回旧失败任务
   104       retry(task.id);
   105       return;
   106     }
   107     if (status === 'completed') {
   108       // 打开文件：APK→安装，其他→系统打开方式
   109       if (task.localUri) openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);
   110       return;
   111     }
   112     if (status === 'downloading') { pause(task.id); return; }
   113     if (status === 'paused') { resume(task.id); return; }
   114     if (status === 'pending') { cancel(task.id); return; }
   115   };
   116 
   117   // ── 已完成 ──────────────────────────────────────────
   118   if (status === 'completed') {
   119     return (
   120       <Pressable
   121         onPress={handlePress}
   122         style={{
   123           paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
   124           paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
   125           borderRadius: 24,
   126           backgroundColor: GREEN,
   127         }}
   128       >
   129         <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FFFFFF' }}>
   130           {isApk ? '安装' : '打开'}
   131         </Text>
   132       </Pressable>
   133     );
   134   }
   135 
   136   // ── 下载中 / 暂停 / 排队 ──────────────────────────
   137   if (task && (status === 'downloading' || status === 'paused' || status === 'pending')) {
   138     const progress = task.progress;
   139     const strokeDashoffset = CIRCUMFERENCE * (1 - progress);
   140     const isPaused = status === 'paused';
   141     const isPending = status === 'pending';
   142     const accentColor = isPaused ? ORANGE : BLUE;
   143 
   144     if (compact) {
   145       return (
   146         <Pressable onPress={handlePress} style={{ alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', width: 48, height: 32 }}>
   147           <Svg width={28} height={28} viewBox="0 0 28 28">
   148             <Circle cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS} stroke="#E0E0E0" strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none" />
   149             {!isPending && (
   150               <Circle
   151                 cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS}
   152                 stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none"
   153                 strokeDasharray={`${CIRCUMFERENCE} ${CIRCUMFERENCE}`}
   154                 strokeDashoffset={strokeDashoffset}
   155                 strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="14,14"
   156               />
   157             )}
   158           </Svg>
   159           <View style={{ position: 'absolute' }}>
   160             <Ionicons
   161               name={isPending ? 'hourglass-outline' : isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'}
   162               size={11} color={accentColor}
   163             />
   164           </View>
   165         </Pressable>
   166       );
   167     }
   168 
   169     const percent = Math.round(progress * 100);
   170     const speedStr = formatSpeed(task.speed);
   171     return (
   172       <Pressable onPress={handlePress} style={{ alignItems: 'center', gap: 4, minWidth: 60 }}>
   173         <View style={{ position: 'relative', width: 44, height: 44 }}>
   174           <Svg width={44} height={44} viewBox="0 0 44 44">
   175             <Circle cx={22} cy={22} r={18} stroke="#E5E5E5" strokeWidth={3} fill="none" />
   176             {!isPending && (
   177               <Circle
   178                 cx={22} cy={22} r={18}
   179                 stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={3} fill="none"
   180                 strokeDasharray={`${2 * Math.PI * 18} ${2 * Math.PI * 18}`}
   181                 strokeDashoffset={(2 * Math.PI * 18) * (1 - progress)}
   182                 strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="22,22"
   183               />
   184             )}
   185           </Svg>
   186           <View style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0, alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
   187             {isPending
   188               ? <Ionicons name="hourglass-outline" size={16} color="#AAAAAA" />
   189               : <Ionicons name={isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'} size={15} color={accentColor} />}
   190           </View>
   191         </View>
   192         <Text style={{ fontSize: 11, color: accentColor, fontWeight: '600' }}>
   193           {isPending ? '等待中' : isPaused ? `${percent}% 已暂停` : `${percent}%`}
   194         </Text>
   195         {speedStr && !isPaused ? <Text style={{ fontSize: 10, color: '#999999' }}>{speedStr}</Text> : null}
   196       </Pressable>
   197     );
   198   }
   199 
   200   // ── 失败 ────────────────────────────────────────────
   201   if (status === 'failed') {
   202     return (
   203       <Pressable
   204         onPress={handlePress}
   205         style={{
   206           paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
   207           paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
   208           borderRadius: 24,
   209           backgroundColor: '#FF4D4F',
   210         }}
   211       >
   212         <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FFFFFF' }}>
   213           重试
   214         </Text>
   215       </Pressable>
   216     );
   217   }
   218 
   219   // ── 初始状态 ─────────────────────────────────────────
   220   return (
   221     <Pressable
   222       onPress={handlePress}
   223       style={{
   224         paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
   225         paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
   226         borderRadius: 24,
   227         borderWidth: 1.5,
   228         borderColor: BLUE,
   229         backgroundColor: '#FFFFFF',
   230       }}
   231     >
   232       <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: BLUE }}>
   233         下载
   234       </Text>
   235     </Pressable>
   236   );

    15 // 内存缓存 SAF 目录 URI；undefined = 尚未初始化，null = 无权限/非 Android
    16 let _safDirUri: string | null | undefined = undefined;
    17 
    18 /** 从 AsyncStorage 恢复上次已授权的 SAF 目录 URI，并验证权限是否仍有效 */
    19 async function loadSafUri(): Promise<string | null> {
    20   if (_safDirUri !== undefined) return _safDirUri;
    21   const stored = await AsyncStorage.getItem(SAF_URI_KEY).catch(() => null);
    22   if (stored) {
    23     try {
    24       await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.readDirectoryAsync(stored);
    25       _safDirUri = stored;
    26       return stored;
    27     } catch {
    28       // 权限被吊销，清除缓存
    29       _safDirUri = null;
    30       await AsyncStorage.removeItem(SAF_URI_KEY).catch(() => null);
    31     }
    32   } else {
    33     _safDirUri = null;
    34   }
    35   return null;
    36 }
    37 
    38 /**
    39  * 弹出系统文件夹选择器，引导用户授权 Download 目录。
    40  * 授权成功后自动在其中创建「开源应用商店」子目录并持久化 URI。
    41  * 返回 true 表示已成功获取目录权限。
    42  */
    43 export async function requestDownloadsPermission(): Promise<boolean> {
    44   if (Platform.OS !== 'android') return false;
    45   try {
    46     // 预设初始路径为 primary:Download，用户只需点「使用此文件夹」即可
    47     const result = await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.requestDirectoryPermissionsAsync(
    48       'content://com.android.externalstorage.documents/tree/primary%3ADownload'
    49     );
    50     if (!result.granted) return false;
    51 
    52     // 尝试在所选目录下创建「开源应用商店」子目录
    53     let finalUri = result.directoryUri;
    54     try {
    55       finalUri = await (FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework as any).makeDirectoryAsync(
    56         result.directoryUri,
    57         APP_FOLDER_NAME
    58       );
    59     } catch {
    60       // makeDirectoryAsync 可能不存在（老版本）或目录已存在，使用父目录
    61     }
    62 
    63     _safDirUri = finalUri;
    64     await AsyncStorage.setItem(SAF_URI_KEY, finalUri).catch(() => null);
    65     return true;
    66   } catch {
    67     return false;
    68   }
    69 }
    70 
    71 /** 清除已保存的 SAF 授权（用于设置页重置） */
    72 export async function resetDownloadsPermission(): Promise<void> {
    73   _safDirUri = null;
    74   await AsyncStorage.removeItem(SAF_URI_KEY).catch(() => null);
    75 }

   119 export type DownloadStatus =
   120   | 'pending'      // 排队等待
   121   | 'downloading'  // 下载中
   122   | 'paused'       // 已暂停
   123   | 'completed'    // 完成
   124   | 'failed'       // 失败
   125   | 'cancelled';   // 已取消
   126 
   127 export interface DownloadTask {
   128   id: string;
   129   url: string;
   130   filename: string;
   131   appId: number;
   132   appName: string;
   133   owner: string;
   134   repo: string;
   135   avatarUrl: string;
   136   version: string;
   137   status: DownloadStatus;
   138   progress: number;       // 0 ~ 1
   139   bytesWritten: number;
   140   totalBytes: number;
   141   speed: number;          // bytes/s
   142   localUri: string | null;
   143   error: string | null;
   144   createdAt: number;
   145 }
   146 
   147 type ProgressCallback = (task: DownloadTask) => void;
   148 
   149 const MAX_CONCURRENT = 3;
   150 
   151 // 任务表：id -> DownloadTask
   152 const tasks = new Map<string, DownloadTask>();
   153 // DownloadResumable 实例表：id -> instance
   154 const resumables = new Map<string, FileSystem.DownloadResumable>();
   155 // 暂停快照：id -> resumeData（Base64），用于真正从断点续传
   156 const resumeSnapshots = new Map<string, string>();
   157 // 上一次收到进度回调的时间戳（用于计算速度）
   158 const lastProgressTime = new Map<string, { ts: number; bytes: number }>();
   159 // 全局订阅者
   160 const subscribers = new Set<ProgressCallback>();
   161 
   162 // 生成唯一 ID
   163 function genId(): string {
   164   return `dl_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7)}`;
   165 }
   166 
   167 // 通知所有订阅者
   168 function notify(task: DownloadTask) {
   169   subscribers.forEach((cb) => cb({ ...task }));
   170 }
   171 
   172 // 从等待队列中取下一个并发槽
   173 function flushQueue() {
   174   const downloading = [...tasks.values()].filter((t) => t.status === 'downloading').length;
   175   if (downloading >= MAX_CONCURRENT) return;
   176 
   177   const next = [...tasks.values()].find((t) => t.status === 'pending');
   178   if (next) startTask(next.id);
   179 }

New String: ```
/** 推断文件 MIME 类型 */
export function getMimeType(filename: string): string {
  const lower = filename.toLowerCase();
  if (lower.endsWith('.apk'))    return 'application/vnd.android.package-archive';
  if (lower.endsWith('.ipa'))    return 'application/octet-stream';
  if (lower.endsWith('.exe'))    return 'application/vnd.microsoft.portable-executable';
  if (lower.endsWith('.msi'))    return 'application/x-msi';
  if (lower.endsWith('.dmg'))    return 'application/x-apple-diskimage';
  if (lower.endsWith('.pkg'))    return 'application/octet-stream';
  if (lower.endsWith('.deb'))    return 'application/vnd.debian.binary-package';
  if (lower.endsWith('.rpm'))    return 'application/x-rpm';
  if (lower.endsWith('.appimage')) return 'application/octet-stream';
  if (lower.endsWith('.zip'))    return 'application/zip';
  if (lower.endsWith('.tar.gz') || lower.endsWith('.tgz')) return 'application/gzip';
  if (lower.endsWith('.tar'))    return 'application/x-tar';
  if (lower.endsWith('.7z'))     return 'application/x-7z-compressed';
  return 'application/octet-stream';
}

/** 判断文件是否为安装包（各平台安装程序格式） */
export function isInstallerFile(filename: string): boolean {
  const lower = filename.toLowerCase();
  return (
    lower.endsWith('.apk') ||   // Android
    lower.endsWith('.ipa') ||   // iOS
    lower.endsWith('.exe') ||   // Windows
    lower.endsWith('.msi') ||   // Windows
    lower.endsWith('.dmg') ||   // macOS
    lower.endsWith('.pkg') ||   // macOS
    lower.endsWith('.deb') ||   // Linux
    lower.endsWith('.rpm') ||   // Linux
    lower.endsWith('.appimage') // Linux
  );
}

/**
 * 验证已下载文件是否有效：文件存在且大小 > 0。
 * content:// SAF URI 无法用 getInfoAsync 校验，默认视为有效。
 * 返回错误描述字符串，null 表示验证通过。
 */
async function validateFile(uri: string): Promise<string | null> {
  // SAF content:// URI 跳过 getInfoAsync（不支持），视为有效
  if (uri.startsWith('content://')) return null;
  try {
    const info = await FileSystem.getInfoAsync(uri);
    if (!info.exists) return '文件不存在，可能已被删除';
    if ((info as any).size === 0) return '文件大小为 0，下载可能不完整';
    return null;
  } catch {
    return null; // 无法获取信息时不阻断流程
  }
}

/**
 * 将已下载到 documentDirectory 的临时文件复制到 SAF Downloads 目录。
 * 成功则返回新的 content:// URI 并删除临时文件；失败则返回原 tempUri。
 */
async function moveToSafDownloads(tempUri: string, filename: string): Promise<string> {
  try {
    const dirUri = await loadSafUri();
    if (!dirUri) return tempUri;

    const mimeType = getMimeType(filename);

    // 在 SAF 目录中创建目标文件（若同名文件已存在，会自动追加编号）
    const destUri = await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.createFileAsync(
      dirUri, filename, mimeType
    );

    // 将 file:// 临时文件复制到 content:// SAF 文件
    await FileSystem.StorageAccessFramework.copyAsync({ from: tempUri, to: destUri });

    // 删除临时文件
    await FileSystem.deleteAsync(tempUri, { idempotent: true }).catch(() => null);

    return destUri;
  } catch {
    // SAF 操作失败，保留临时文件路径，不影响下载结果
    return tempUri;
  }
}
```

New String: ```
  try {
    const result = await resumable.downloadAsync();
    const t = tasks.get(id);
    if (!t) return;

    if (result) {
      // 验证文件有效性（存在且大小 > 0）
      const validErr = await validateFile(result.uri);
      if (validErr) {
        t.status = 'failed';
        t.error = validErr;
        notify(t);
        return;
      }

      t.status = 'completed';
      t.progress = 1;
      t.speed = 0;
      // Android：将临时文件移到 SAF Downloads/开源应用商店/，非 Android 直接用原路径
      if (Platform.OS === 'android') {
        t.localUri = await moveToSafDownloads(result.uri, task.filename);
        // 清理空的临时目录
        await FileSystem.deleteAsync(dir, { idempotent: true }).catch(() => null);
      } else {
        t.localUri = result.uri;
      }
    } else {
      // 已被取消
      if (t.status !== 'cancelled') {
        t.status = 'cancelled';
      }
    }
    notify(t);
  } catch (e: any) {
    const t = tasks.get(id);
    if (!t) return;
    if (t.status !== 'cancelled' && t.status !== 'paused') {
      t.status = 'failed';
      // 将常见网络错误转换为用户可读描述
      const msg: string = e?.message ?? '';
      if (msg.includes('Network request failed') || msg.includes('Unable to resolve host')) {
        t.error = '网络连接失败，请检查网络后重试';
      } else if (msg.includes('No space left') || msg.includes('ENOSPC')) {
        t.error = '存储空间不足，请清理设备空间后重试';
      } else if (msg.includes('403') || msg.includes('Forbidden')) {
        t.error = '下载链接无权访问（403），请重新获取';
      } else if (msg.includes('404') || msg.includes('Not Found')) {
        t.error = '文件不存在（404），该版本可能已删除';
      } else if (msg.includes('timeout') || msg.includes('ETIMEDOUT')) {
        t.error = '下载超时，请检查网络连接后重试';
      } else {
        t.error = msg || '下载失败，请重试';
      }
      notify(t);
    }
  } finally {
    resumables.delete(id);
    lastProgressTime.delete(id);
    flushQueue();
  }
```
