```
/**
 * 下载进度按钮
 * 状态：初始 → 下载中（进度圆弧 + 速度）→ 完成 → 打开/安装
 * - APK 文件：完成后显示「安装」，调起 Android 系统包安装器
 * - 其他文件：完成后显示「打开」，调起系统分享/打开方式对话框
 * - 重试：先清除旧失败任务再重新入队，彻底解决重试无效问题
 */
import { View, Text, Pressable, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import Svg, { Circle } from 'react-native-svg';
import { Ionicons } from '@expo/vector-icons';
import * as Sharing from 'expo-sharing';
import { useDownload } from '@/ctx/DownloadContext';
import { formatSpeed } from '@/lib/downloadManager';
import type { DownloadTask } from '@/lib/downloadManager';

interface Props {
  downloadUrl: string;
  filename: string;
  appId: number;
  appName: string;
  owner: string;
  repo: string;
  avatarUrl: string;
  version: string;
  /** 紧凑模式：用于 AppCard 列表场景 */
  compact?: boolean;
}

const BLUE = '#1677FF';
const GREEN = '#52C41A';
const ORANGE = '#FA8C16';
const RADIUS = 11;
const CIRCUMFERENCE = 2 * Math.PI * RADIUS;

/** 判断文件是否为 APK 安装包 */
function isApkFile(filename: string): boolean {
  return filename.toLowerCase().endsWith('.apk');
}

/** 根据文件名推断 MIME 类型，用于 expo-sharing */
function getMimeType(filename: string): string {
  const lower = filename.toLowerCase();
  if (lower.endsWith('.apk')) return 'application/vnd.android.package-archive';
  if (lower.endsWith('.zip')) return 'application/zip';
  if (lower.endsWith('.tar.gz') || lower.endsWith('.tgz')) return 'application/gzip';
  if (lower.endsWith('.deb')) return 'application/vnd.debian.binary-package';
  if (lower.endsWith('.rpm')) return 'application/x-rpm';
  if (lower.endsWith('.dmg') || lower.endsWith('.pkg')) return 'application/octet-stream';
  if (lower.endsWith('.exe') || lower.endsWith('.msi')) return 'application/octet-stream';
  if (lower.endsWith('.appimage')) return 'application/octet-stream';
  if (lower.endsWith('.ipa')) return 'application/octet-stream';
  return 'application/octet-stream';
}

/** 打开已下载的文件：APK 触发安装，其他文件调起系统「打开方式」 */
async function openLocalFile(localUri: string, filename: string) {
  // Web 平台：无本地文件，无法 sharing
  if (Platform.OS === 'web') return;
  try {
    const mimeType = getMimeType(filename);
    const available = await Sharing.isAvailableAsync();
    if (available) {
      await Sharing.shareAsync(localUri, { mimeType, dialogTitle: '打开文件' });
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.warn('openLocalFile error:', e);
  }
}

export default function DownloadProgressButton({
  downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version,
  compact = false,
}: Props) {
  const { enqueue, retry, pause, resume, cancel, findByUrl } = useDownload();
  const task: DownloadTask | undefined = findByUrl(downloadUrl);
  const status = task?.status;
  const isApk = isApkFile(filename);

  // 下载完成后自动调起安装器（仅 Android APK）
  // 初始值：若挂载时任务已完成则置 true，避免页面切换回来时重复弹窗
  const autoInstallFiredRef = useRef(task?.status === 'completed');
  useEffect(() => {
    if (
      status === 'completed' &&
      task?.localUri &&
      isApk &&
      Platform.OS === 'android' &&
      !autoInstallFiredRef.current
    ) {
      autoInstallFiredRef.current = true;
      openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);
    }
  }, [status, task?.localUri, isApk, filename]);

  const handlePress = () => {
    if (!task || status === 'cancelled') {
      // 全新下载
      enqueue({ url: downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version });
      return;
    }
    if (status === 'failed') {
      // 重试：通过 retry(id) 先删除旧任务再重新入队，避免 findByUrl 返回旧失败任务
      retry(task.id);
      return;
    }
    if (status === 'completed') {
      // 打开文件：APK→安装，其他→系统打开方式
      if (task.localUri) openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);
      return;
    }
    if (status === 'downloading') { pause(task.id); return; }
    if (status === 'paused') { resume(task.id); return; }
    if (status === 'pending') { cancel(task.id); return; }
  };

  // ── 已完成 ──────────────────────────────────────────
  if (status === 'completed') {
    return (
      <Pressable
        onPress={handlePress}
        style={{
          paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
          paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
          borderRadius: 24,
          backgroundColor: GREEN,
        }}
      >
        <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FFFFFF' }}>
          {isApk ? '安装' : '打开'}
        </Text>
      </Pressable>
    );
  }

  // ── 下载中 / 暂停 / 排队 ──────────────────────────
  if (task && (status === 'downloading' || status === 'paused' || status === 'pending')) {
    const progress = task.progress;
    const strokeDashoffset = CIRCUMFERENCE * (1 - progress);
    const isPaused = status === 'paused';
    const isPending = status === 'pending';
    const accentColor = isPaused ? ORANGE : BLUE;

    if (compact) {
      return (
        <Pressable onPress={handlePress} style={{ alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', width: 48, height: 32 }}>
          <Svg width={28} height={28} viewBox="0 0 28 28">
            <Circle cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS} stroke="#E0E0E0" strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none" />
            {!isPending && (
              <Circle
                cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS}
                stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none"
                strokeDasharray={`${CIRCUMFERENCE} ${CIRCUMFERENCE}`}
                strokeDashoffset={strokeDashoffset}
                strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="14,14"
              />
            )}
          </Svg>
          <View style={{ position: 'absolute' }}>
            <Ionicons
              name={isPending ? 'hourglass-outline' : isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'}
              size={11} color={accentColor}
            />
          </View>
        </Pressable>
      );
    }

    const percent = Math.round(progress * 100);
    const speedStr = formatSpeed(task.speed);
    return (
      <Pressable onPress={handlePress} style={{ alignItems: 'center', gap: 4, minWidth: 60 }}>
        <View style={{ position: 'relative', width: 44, height: 44 }}>
          <Svg width={44} height={44} viewBox="0 0 44 44">
            <Circle cx={22} cy={22} r={18} stroke="#E5E5E5" strokeWidth={3} fill="none" />
            {!isPending && (
              <Circle
                cx={22} cy={22} r={18}
                stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={3} fill="none"
                strokeDasharray={`${2 * Math.PI * 18} ${2 * Math.PI * 18}`}
                strokeDashoffset={(2 * Math.PI * 18) * (1 - progress)}
                strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="22,22"
              />
            )}
          </Svg>
          <View style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0, alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
            {isPending
              ? <Ionicons name="hourglass-outline" size={16} color="#AAAAAA" />
              : <Ionicons name={isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'} size={15} color={accentColor} />}
          </View>
        </View>
        <Text style={{ fontSize: 11, color: accentColor, fontWeight: '600' }}>
          {isPending ? '等待中' : isPaused ? `${percent}% 已暂停` : `${percent}%`}
        </Text>
        {speedStr && !isPaused ? <Text style={{ fontSize: 10, color: '#999999' }}>{speedStr}</Text> : null}
      </Pressable>
    );
  }

  // ── 失败 ────────────────────────────────────────────
  if (status === 'failed') {
    return (
      <Pressable
        onPress={handlePress}
        style={{
          paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
          paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
          borderRadius: 24,
          backgroundColor: '#FF4D4F',
        }}
      >
        <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FFFFFF' }}>
          重试
        </Text>
      </Pressable>
    );
  }

  // ── 初始状态 ─────────────────────────────────────────
  return (
    <Pressable
      onPress={handlePress}
      style={{
        paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
        paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
        borderRadius: 24,
        borderWidth: 1.5,
        borderColor: BLUE,
        backgroundColor: '#FFFFFF',
      }}
    >
      <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: BLUE }}>
        下载
      </Text>
    </Pressable>
  );
}
```
New String: ```
/**
 * 下载进度按钮
 * 状态：初始 → 下载中（进度圆弧 + 速度）→ 完成 → 安装/查看
 * - 安装包（APK/IPA/EXE/MSI/DMG/DEB/RPM/AppImage）：显示「安装」，调起系统安装器
 *   · Android APK 下载完成后自动弹出安装器
 * - 其他文件：显示「查看」，调起系统推荐打开方式
 * - 失败：显示错误摘要 + 重试按钮
 * - 重试：清除旧任务再重新入队，彻底解决重试无效问题
 */
import { View, Text, Pressable, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import Svg, { Circle } from 'react-native-svg';
import { Ionicons } from '@expo/vector-icons';
import * as Sharing from 'expo-sharing';
import { useDownload } from '@/ctx/DownloadContext';
import { formatSpeed, getMimeType, isInstallerFile } from '@/lib/downloadManager';
import type { DownloadTask } from '@/lib/downloadManager';

interface Props {
  downloadUrl: string;
  filename: string;
  appId: number;
  appName: string;
  owner: string;
  repo: string;
  avatarUrl: string;
  version: string;
  /** 紧凑模式：用于 AppCard 列表场景 */
  compact?: boolean;
}

const BLUE   = '#1677FF';
const GREEN  = '#52C41A';
const ORANGE = '#FA8C16';
const RED    = '#FF4D4F';
const RADIUS = 11;
const CIRCUMFERENCE = 2 * Math.PI * RADIUS;

/**
 * 打开 / 安装已下载的文件。
 * - 安装包：调起系统安装器（shareAsync 会路由到包安装器）
 * - 其他文件：调起系统推荐的打开应用
 * 返回成功与否及错误描述。
 */
async function openLocalFile(
  localUri: string,
  filename: string
): Promise<{ ok: boolean; error?: string }> {
  if (Platform.OS === 'web') return { ok: false, error: 'Web 平台不支持本地文件操作' };
  if (!localUri) return { ok: false, error: '文件路径无效' };
  try {
    const mimeType = getMimeType(filename);
    const available = await Sharing.isAvailableAsync();
    if (!available) return { ok: false, error: '当前设备不支持文件分享/打开' };
    await Sharing.shareAsync(localUri, {
      mimeType,
      dialogTitle: isInstallerFile(filename) ? '安装应用' : '查看文件',
    });
    return { ok: true };
  } catch (e: any) {
    const msg: string = e?.message ?? '';
    if (msg.includes('No Activity') || msg.includes('no activity')) {
      return { ok: false, error: '未找到可处理该文件的应用' };
    }
    if (msg.includes('Permission') || msg.includes('permission')) {
      return { ok: false, error: '权限不足，无法访问文件' };
    }
    return { ok: false, error: '无法打开文件，请检查文件是否存在' };
  }
}

export default function DownloadProgressButton({
  downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version,
  compact = false,
}: Props) {
  const { enqueue, retry, pause, resume, cancel, findByUrl } = useDownload();
  const task: DownloadTask | undefined = findByUrl(downloadUrl);
  const status = task?.status;
  const isInstaller = isInstallerFile(filename);

  // 文件打开失败时的内联错误提示
  const [openError, setOpenError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // 下载完成后自动调起安装器（仅 Android APK）
  // 初始值：若挂载时任务已完成则置 true，避免页面切换回来时重复弹窗
  const autoInstallFiredRef = useRef(task?.status === 'completed');
  useEffect(() => {
    if (
      status === 'completed' &&
      task?.localUri &&
      filename.toLowerCase().endsWith('.apk') &&
      Platform.OS === 'android' &&
      !autoInstallFiredRef.current
    ) {
      autoInstallFiredRef.current = true;
      openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename).then(({ ok, error }) => {
        if (!ok && error) setOpenError(error);
      });
    }
  }, [status, task?.localUri, filename]);

  const handlePress = async () => {
    setOpenError(null);
    if (!task || status === 'cancelled') {
      enqueue({ url: downloadUrl, filename, appId, appName, owner, repo, avatarUrl, version });
      return;
    }
    if (status === 'failed') {
      retry(task.id);
      return;
    }
    if (status === 'completed') {
      if (task.localUri) {
        const { ok, error } = await openLocalFile(task.localUri, filename);
        if (!ok && error) setOpenError(error);
      } else {
        setOpenError('文件路径丢失，请重新下载');
      }
      return;
    }
    if (status === 'downloading') { pause(task.id); return; }
    if (status === 'paused')      { resume(task.id); return; }
    if (status === 'pending')     { cancel(task.id); return; }
  };

  // ── 已完成 ──────────────────────────────────────────
  if (status === 'completed') {
    return (
      <View style={{ alignItems: 'flex-end', gap: 4 }}>
        <Pressable
          onPress={handlePress}
          style={{
            paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
            paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
            borderRadius: 24,
            backgroundColor: GREEN,
          }}
        >
          <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FFFFFF' }}>
            {isInstaller ? '安装' : '查看'}
          </Text>
        </Pressable>
        {openError && (
          <Text style={{ fontSize: 10, color: RED, maxWidth: 120, textAlign: 'right' }}>
            {openError}
          </Text>
        )}
      </View>
    );
  }

  // ── 下载中 / 暂停 / 排队 ──────────────────────────
  if (task && (status === 'downloading' || status === 'paused' || status === 'pending')) {
    const progress = task.progress;
    const strokeDashoffset = CIRCUMFERENCE * (1 - progress);
    const isPaused  = status === 'paused';
    const isPending = status === 'pending';
    const accentColor = isPaused ? ORANGE : BLUE;

    if (compact) {
      return (
        <Pressable
          onPress={handlePress}
          style={{ alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', width: 48, height: 32 }}
        >
          <Svg width={28} height={28} viewBox="0 0 28 28">
            <Circle cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS} stroke="#E0E0E0" strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none" />
            {!isPending && (
              <Circle
                cx={14} cy={14} r={RADIUS}
                stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={2.5} fill="none"
                strokeDasharray={`${CIRCUMFERENCE} ${CIRCUMFERENCE}`}
                strokeDashoffset={strokeDashoffset}
                strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="14,14"
              />
            )}
          </Svg>
          <View style={{ position: 'absolute' }}>
            <Ionicons
              name={isPending ? 'hourglass-outline' : isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'}
              size={11} color={accentColor}
            />
          </View>
        </Pressable>
      );
    }

    const percent   = Math.round(progress * 100);
    const speedStr  = formatSpeed(task.speed);
    return (
      <Pressable onPress={handlePress} style={{ alignItems: 'center', gap: 4, minWidth: 60 }}>
        <View style={{ position: 'relative', width: 44, height: 44 }}>
          <Svg width={44} height={44} viewBox="0 0 44 44">
            <Circle cx={22} cy={22} r={18} stroke="#E5E5E5" strokeWidth={3} fill="none" />
            {!isPending && (
              <Circle
                cx={22} cy={22} r={18}
                stroke={accentColor} strokeWidth={3} fill="none"
                strokeDasharray={`${2 * Math.PI * 18} ${2 * Math.PI * 18}`}
                strokeDashoffset={(2 * Math.PI * 18) * (1 - progress)}
                strokeLinecap="round" rotation={-90} origin="22,22"
              />
            )}
          </Svg>
          <View style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0, alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
            {isPending
              ? <Ionicons name="hourglass-outline" size={16} color="#AAAAAA" />
              : <Ionicons name={isPaused ? 'play' : 'pause'} size={15} color={accentColor} />}
          </View>
        </View>
        <Text style={{ fontSize: 11, color: accentColor, fontWeight: '600' }}>
          {isPending ? '等待中' : isPaused ? `${percent}% 已暂停` : `${percent}%`}
        </Text>
        {speedStr && !isPaused
          ? <Text style={{ fontSize: 10, color: '#999999' }}>{speedStr}</Text>
          : null}
      </Pressable>
    );
  }

  // ── 失败 ────────────────────────────────────────────
  if (status === 'failed') {
    return (
      <View style={{ alignItems: 'flex-end', gap: 4 }}>
        <Pressable
          onPress={handlePress}
          style={{
            paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
            paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
            borderRadius: 24,
            backgroundColor: RED,
          }}
        >
          <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FFFFFF' }}>
            重试
          </Text>
        </Pressable>
        {/* 失败原因摘要（最多 2 行，超出省略） */}
        {task?.error && (
          <Text
            numberOfLines={2}
            style={{ fontSize: 10, color: RED, maxWidth: compact ? 90 : 130, textAlign: 'right' }}
          >
            {task.error}
          </Text>
        )}
      </View>
    );
  }

  // ── 初始状态 ─────────────────────────────────────────
  return (
    <Pressable
      onPress={handlePress}
      style={{
        paddingHorizontal: compact ? 12 : 16,
        paddingVertical: compact ? 6 : 9,
        borderRadius: 24,
        borderWidth: 1.5,
        borderColor: BLUE,
        backgroundColor: '#FFFFFF',
      }}
    >
      <Text style={{ fontSize: compact ? 12 : 13, fontWeight: '600', color: BLUE }}>
        下载
      </Text>
    </Pressable>
  );
}
```

     2 import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, FlatList, ScrollView, ActivityIndicator, useWindowDimensions } from 'react-native';
     3 import { useCallback, useRef, useState } from 'react';
     4 import { useFocusEffect, useLocalSearchParams } from 'expo-router';

     6 import { X } from 'lucide-react-native';

     9 import { addSearchHistory, clearSearchHistory, getSearchHistory } from '@/lib/database';
    10 import type { AppItem } from '@/types';
    11 import AppCard from '@/components/openappstore/AppCard';

    14 const HOT_SEARCHES = ['VLC', 'Telegram', 'OBS', 'Signal', 'Termux', 'Syncthing', 'Bitwarden', 'Kodi', 'Neovim', 'FFmpeg'];
    15 
    16 function useResponsive() {
    17   const { width } = useWindowDimensions();
    18   const isWide = width >= 600;
    19   const contentWidth = isWide ? Math.min(width, 720) : width;
    20   const hPad = isWide ? 24 : 16;
    21   return { isWide, contentWidth, hPad };
    22 }
    23 
    24 export default function SearchTab() {
    25   const inputRef = useRef<TextInput>(null);
    26   // 非受控：textRef 持有实时文本，不触发 re-render，彻底解决 Android 光标跳末尾
    27   const textRef = useRef('');
    28   // 仅控制清除按钮显隐，不绑定到 TextInput value
    29   const [hasText, setHasText] = useState(false);
    30 
    31   const [history, setHistory] = useState<string[]>([]);
    32   const [results, setResults] = useState<AppItem[]>([]);
    33   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
    34   const [searched, setSearched] = useState(false);
    35   const [searchError, setSearchError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    36   const { isWide, contentWidth, hPad } = useResponsive();
    37   const { focus } = useLocalSearchParams<{ focus?: string }>();
    38 
    39   const loadHistory = useCallback(async () => {
    40     const h = await getSearchHistory();
    41     setHistory(h);
    42   }, []);
    43 
    44   useFocusEffect(useCallback(() => {
    45     loadHistory();
    46     if (focus === '1') {
    47       const timer = setTimeout(() => inputRef.current?.focus(), 320);
    48       return () => clearTimeout(timer);
    49     }
    50   }, [loadHistory, focus]));
    51 
    52   const handleChangeText = useCallback((text: string) => {
    53     textRef.current = text;
    54     setHasText(text.length > 0);
    55   }, []);
    56 
    57   /** 清除输入框：用 setNativeProps 避免销毁/重建 TextInput */
    58   const clearInput = useCallback(() => {
    59     inputRef.current?.clear();
    60     textRef.current = '';
    61     setHasText(false);
    62   }, []);
    63 
    64   const performSearch = async (keyword: string) => {
    65     const kw = keyword.trim();
    66     if (!kw) return;
    67     inputRef.current?.blur();
    68     // 写历史记录不阻塞搜索，OPFS 冲突等 DB 错误不应影响搜索功能
    69     addSearchHistory(kw).catch(() => null);
    70     setHistory((prev) => [kw, ...prev.filter((k) => k !== kw)].slice(0, 20));
    71     try {
    72       setLoading(true);
    73       setSearched(true);
    74       setSearchError(null);
    75       const { items } = await searchRepos(`${kw} stars:>10`, { sort: 'stars', per_page: 30 });
    76       setResults(items);
    77     } catch (e: any) {
    78       const msg: string = e?.message || '搜索失败，请稍后重试';
    79       if (msg.includes('403') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('rate limit') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('secondary')) {
    80         setSearchError('API 请求超限（匿名每小时 10 次），请在「我的」页面配置 GitHub Token 以提高限额');
    81       } else if (msg.includes('422')) {
    82         setSearchError('搜索关键词格式有误，请换个词试试');
    83       } else if (msg.toLowerCase().includes('network') || msg.toLowerCase().includes('fetch')) {
    84         setSearchError('网络连接失败，请检查网络后重试');
    85       } else {
    86         setSearchError(`搜索失败：${msg}`);
    87       }
    88       setResults([]);
    89     } finally {
    90       setLoading(false);
    91     }
    92   };
    93 
    94   /** 点击历史/热门词：直接触发搜索，不依赖 setNativeProps（Web 不可靠） */
    95   const searchFromTag = (kw: string) => {
    96     textRef.current = kw;
    97     setHasText(true);
    98     // setNativeProps 在 Web 上不可靠，改为在 performSearch 后让 input 通过 defaultValue 刷新
    99     // 直接传 kw 给 performSearch，不依赖 input DOM 状态
   100     performSearch(kw);
   101   };
   102 
   103   const handleClearHistory = async () => {
   104     await clearSearchHistory();
   105     setHistory([]);
   106   };
   107 
   108   const handleCancel = () => {
   109     setSearched(false);
   110     clearInput();
   111     setResults([]);
   112     setSearchError(null);
   113     inputRef.current?.blur();
   114   };
   115 
   116   const tagStyle = {
   117     paddingHorizontal: 13,
   118     paddingVertical: 6,
   119     borderRadius: 20,
   120     borderWidth: 1,
   121     borderColor: '#E8E8E8',
   122     backgroundColor: '#FFFFFF',
   123   };
   124 
   125   const centerWrap = isWide ? { alignItems: 'center' as const } : {};
   126   const innerWrap = isWide ? { width: contentWidth } : {};
   127 
   128   return (
   129     <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#F5F5F5' }} edges={['top']}>
   130       {/* Android 已设 softwareKeyboardLayoutMode=pan，不需要 KAV，避免高度重算抖动 */}
   131       <View style={{ flex: 1 }}>
   132         {/* ── 搜索框：非受控模式，永不绑定 value，彻底消除光标跳末尾 ── */}
   133         <View style={centerWrap}>
   134           <View style={[innerWrap, {
   135             flexDirection: 'row',
   136             alignItems: 'center',
   137             paddingHorizontal: hPad,

   140             gap: 10,

   142             <View style={{
   143               flex: 1,

   145               alignItems: 'center',
   146               backgroundColor: '#FFFFFF',
   147               borderRadius: 12,

   149               // 用固定高度代替 paddingVertical，防止 Web 聚焦时 outline/border 撑高搜索框
   150               height: 42,
   151               boxShadow: [{ offsetX: 0, offsetY: 1, blurRadius: 3, color: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)' }],
   152             } as any}>
   153               <Ionicons name="search-outline" size={16} color="#AAAAAA" />
   154               <TextInput
   155                 ref={inputRef}

   161                   lineHeight: 20,
   162                   color: '#1A1A1A',
   163                   // Web: 消除聚焦时的 outline 和 border（这两者会撑高搜索框）
   164                   outlineWidth: 0,
   165                   outlineStyle: 'none',
   166                   borderWidth: 0,
   167                 } as any}
   168                 placeholder="搜索开源应用…"
   169                 placeholderTextColor="#AAAAAA"
   170                 // 故意不传 value — 非受控，Android 不会重置光标
   171                 onChangeText={handleChangeText}
   172                 onSubmitEditing={() => performSearch(textRef.current)}
   173                 returnKeyType="search"
   174                 underlineColorAndroid="transparent"
   175                 blurOnSubmit={false}
   176               />
   177               {hasText && (
   178                 <Pressable onPress={clearInput} style={{ padding: 2 }} hitSlop={8}>
   179                   <X size={15} color="#AAAAAA" />
   180                 </Pressable>
   181               )}
   182             </View>
   183             {searched && (
   184               <Pressable onPress={handleCancel} style={{ paddingVertical: 4 }} hitSlop={8}>
   185                 <Text style={{ fontSize: 15, color: '#1677FF' }}>取消</Text>
   186               </Pressable>
   187             )}
   188           </View>
   189         </View>
   190 
   191         {/* ── 内容区 ── */}
   192         {!searched ? (
   193           // 预搜索区：用 ScrollView 替代 FlatList(data=[])
   194           // FlatList 内部手势识别会延迟 onPress（判断是否为滚动），ScrollView 无此问题
   195           <ScrollView
   196             keyboardShouldPersistTaps="handled"
   197             contentContainerStyle={[
   198               { paddingTop: 6, paddingBottom: 32 },
   199               isWide ? { alignItems: 'center' } : undefined,
   200             ]}
   201           >
   202             <View style={{ width: isWide ? contentWidth : undefined }}>
   203               {history.length > 0 && (
   204                 <View style={{ paddingHorizontal: hPad, marginBottom: 20 }}>
   205                   <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 10 }}>
   206                     <Text style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: '700', color: '#1A1A1A' }}>搜索历史</Text>
   207                     <Pressable onPress={handleClearHistory} hitSlop={8}>
   208                       <Text style={{ fontSize: 13, color: '#999999' }}>清空</Text>
   209                     </Pressable>
   210                   </View>
   211                   <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: 8 }}>
   212                     {history.map((item) => (
   213                       <Pressable key={item} onPress={() => searchFromTag(item)} style={tagStyle}>
   214                         <Text style={{ fontSize: 13, color: '#333333' }}>{item}</Text>
   215                       </Pressable>
   216                     ))}
   217                   </View>
   218                 </View>
   219               )}
   220               <View style={{ paddingHorizontal: hPad }}>
   221                 <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 10, gap: 5 }}>
   222                   <Text style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: '700', color: '#1A1A1A' }}>热门搜索</Text>
   223                   <Ionicons name="flame" size={16} color="#FF4D00" />
   224                 </View>
   225                 <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: 8 }}>
   226                   {HOT_SEARCHES.map((item) => (
   227                     <Pressable key={item} onPress={() => searchFromTag(item)} style={tagStyle}>
   228                       <Text style={{ fontSize: 13, color: '#333333' }}>{item}</Text>
   229                     </Pressable>
   230                   ))}
   231                 </View>
   232               </View>
   233             </View>
   234           </ScrollView>
   235         ) : loading ? (
   236           <View style={{ flex: 1, alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
   237             <ActivityIndicator color="#1677FF" size="large" />
   238           </View>
   239         ) : searchError ? (
   240           <View style={centerWrap}>
   241             <View style={[innerWrap, {
   242               margin: hPad, padding: 16, borderRadius: 14,
   243               backgroundColor: '#FFF2F0', borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#FFCCC7',
   244             }]}>
   245               <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, marginBottom: 6 }}>
   246                 <Ionicons name="warning-outline" size={18} color="#FF4D4F" />
   247                 <Text style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: '600', color: '#FF4D4F' }}>搜索失败</Text>
   248               </View>
   249               <Text style={{ fontSize: 13, color: '#7A0000', lineHeight: 20 }}>{searchError}</Text>
   250             </View>
   251           </View>
   252         ) : (
   253           <FlatList
   254             data={results}
   255             keyExtractor={(item) => item.id.toString()}
   256             keyboardShouldPersistTaps="handled"
   257             renderItem={({ item }) => (
   258               <View style={centerWrap}>
   259                 <View style={innerWrap}>
   260                   <AppCard app={item} />
   261                 </View>
   262               </View>
   263             )}
   264             ListEmptyComponent={<EmptyState title="未找到相关应用" />}
   265             contentContainerStyle={{ paddingBottom: 24, paddingTop: 6 }}
   266             contentInsetAdjustmentBehavior="automatic"
   267           />
   268         )}
   269       </View>
   270     </SafeAreaView>
   271   );
   272 }
   273 


</observation>

     1 import { supabase } from '@/client/supabase'
     2 import type { AppItem, GitHubRelease } from '@/types'
     3 
     4 let cachedToken: string | null = null
     5 
     6 export async function setGitHubToken(token: string | null) {
     7   cachedToken = token
     8 }
     9 
    10 export async function getGitHubToken(): Promise<string | null> {
    11   return cachedToken
    12 }
    13 
    14 /** 从 supabase.functions.invoke 的 error 中提取可读错误信息 */
    15 async function extractErrorMessage(error: any): Promise<string> {
    16   try {
    17     const raw = await error?.context?.text?.()
    18     if (raw) {
    19       const parsed = JSON.parse(raw)
    20       // Edge Function 返回: { error, details } 或 { message }
    21       if (parsed?.details) return String(parsed.details)
    22       if (parsed?.error) return String(parsed.error)
    23       if (parsed?.message) return String(parsed.message)
    24       return raw
    25     }
    26   } catch { /* ignore parse errors */ }
    27   return error?.message || '请求失败，请稍后重试'
    28 }
    29 
    30 export async function searchRepos(
    31   q: string,
    32   options: { sort?: string; order?: string; page?: number; per_page?: number } = {}
    33 ): Promise<{ items: AppItem[]; total_count: number }> {
    34   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
    35     body: {
    36       action: 'search',
    37       params: { q, sort: options.sort || 'stars', order: options.order || 'desc', page: options.page || 1, per_page: options.per_page || 30 },
    38       token: cachedToken,
    39     },
    40   })
    41   if (error) {
    42     const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
    43     throw new Error(msg)
    44   }
    45   const items = (data.data?.items || []).map((item: any) => mapRepoToApp(item))
    46   return { items, total_count: data.data?.total_count || 0 }
    47 }
    48 
    49 export async function fetchRepoDetail(owner: string, repo: string): Promise<AppItem> {
    50   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
    51     body: {
    52       action: 'repo',
    53       params: { owner, repo },
    54       token: cachedToken,
    55     },
    56   })
    57   if (error) {
    58     const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
    59     throw new Error(msg)
    60   }
    61   return mapRepoToApp(data.data)
    62 }
    63 
    64 export async function fetchReleases(owner: string, repo: string, page = 1): Promise<GitHubRelease[]> {
    65   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
    66     body: {
    67       action: 'releases',
    68       params: { owner, repo, page },
    69       token: cachedToken,
    70     },
    71   })
    72   if (error) {
    73     const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
    74     throw new Error(msg)
    75   }
    76   return (data.data || []).map((r: any) => ({
    77     id: r.id,
    78     tag_name: r.tag_name,
    79     name: r.name || r.tag_name,
    80     body: r.body,
    81     published_at: r.published_at,
    82     html_url: r.html_url,
    83     assets: (r.assets || []).map((a: any) => ({
    84       name: a.name,
    85       size: a.size,
    86       download_count: a.download_count || 0,
    87       browser_download_url: a.browser_download_url,
    88     })),
    89   }))
    90 }
    91 
    92 export async function fetchReadme(owner: string, repo: string): Promise<string> {
    93   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
    94     body: {
    95       action: 'readme',
    96       params: { owner, repo },
    97       token: cachedToken,
    98     },
    99   })
   100   if (error) {
   101     const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
   102     throw new Error(msg)
   103   }
   104   // GitHub API 返回的 base64 中含 `\n`，必须先清除再 atob
   105   const raw = (data.data?.content || '').replace(/\s/g, '')
   106   if (!raw) return ''
   107   try {
   108     // 优先使用 TextDecoder 正确处理多字节 UTF-8 字符（中文、emoji 等）
   109     const bytes = Uint8Array.from(atob(raw), (c) => c.charCodeAt(0))
   110     return new TextDecoder().decode(bytes)
   111   } catch {
   112     try {
   113       // 降级方案：旧浏览器 / 纯 ASCII README
   114       return decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(raw)))
   115     } catch {
   116       return ''
   117     }
   118   }
   119 }
   120 
   121 export async function fetchContributors(owner: string, repo: string): Promise<Array<{ login: string; avatar_url: string; html_url: string }>> {
   122   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
   123     body: {

   127     },
   128   })
   129   if (error) {
   130     const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
   131     throw new Error(msg)
   132   }

   134     login: c.login,
   135     avatar_url: c.avatar_url,

   137   }))
   138 }

   140 export async function fetchRateLimit(): Promise<{ remaining: number; limit: number; reset: number }> {
   141   const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('github-proxy', {
   142     body: {
   143       action: 'rate_limit',
   144       token: cachedToken,
   145     },
   146   })
   147   if (error) {
   148     const msg = await extractErrorMessage(error)
   149     throw new Error(msg)
   150   }
   151   const core = data.data?.resources?.core || data.data?.rate || { remaining: 0, limit: 60, reset: 0 }
   152   return {
   153     remaining: core.remaining ?? 0,
   154     limit: core.limit ?? 60,
   155     reset: core.reset ?? 0,
   156   }

   159 function mapRepoToApp(item: any): AppItem {
   160   const platforms = detectPlatforms(item.topics || [])
   161   return {
   162     id: item.id,
   163     full_name: item.full_name,
   164     name: item.name,
   165     description: item.description,
   166     owner: item.owner?.login || '',
   167     repo: item.name,
   168     avatar_url: item.owner?.avatar_url || '',
   169     stars: item.stargazers_count || 0,
   170     forks: item.forks_count || 0,
   171     language: item.language,
   172     topics: item.topics || [],
   173     platforms,
   174     latest_version: null,
   175     latest_release_date: null,
   176     html_url: item.html_url,
   177     updated_at: item.updated_at || item.pushed_at,
   178   }
   179 }
   180 
   181 function detectPlatforms(topics: string[]): string[] {
   182   const map: Record<string, string> = {
   183     'android-app': 'Android',
   184     'android': 'Android',
   185     'ios-app': 'iOS',
   186     'ios': 'iOS',
   187     'macos': 'macOS',
   188     'macos-app': 'macOS',
   189     'windows': 'Windows',
   190     'windows-app': 'Windows',
   191     'linux': 'Linux',
   192     'linux-app': 'Linux',
   193     'electron': 'Windows',
   194     'cross-platform': 'Android',
   195   }
   196   const platforms = new Set<string>()
   197   for (const topic of topics) {
   198     const lower = topic.toLowerCase()
   199     if (map[lower]) platforms.add(map[lower])
   200   }
   201   return Array.from(platforms)
   202 }
   203 
   204 export function getPlatformFromFilename(filename: string): string | null {
   205   const lower = filename.toLowerCase()
   206   if (lower.endsWith('.apk')) return 'Android'
   207   if (lower.endsWith('.ipa')) return 'iOS'
   208   if (lower.endsWith('.dmg')) return 'macOS'
   209   if (lower.endsWith('.exe') || lower.endsWith('.msi')) return 'Windows'
   210   if (lower.endsWith('.deb') || lower.endsWith('.rpm') || lower.endsWith('.appimage')) return 'Linux'
   211   return null
   212 }
   213 
   214 export function filterInstallAssets(assets: GitHubRelease['assets']) {
   215   const sigExts = ['.asc', '.sig', '.sha256', '.sha512', '.md5', '.txt']
   216   return assets.filter((a) => {
   217     const lower = a.name.toLowerCase()
   218     return !sigExts.some((ext) => lower.endsWith(ext))
   219   })
   220 }

    17 function stripBadges(md: string): string {
    18   return md
    19     .split('\n')
    20     .filter((line) => {
    21       const lower = line.trim().toLowerCase();
    22       const badgeDomains = [
    23         'shields.io', 'img.shields.io', 'badge.fury.io', 'travis-ci',
    24         'codecov.io', 'coveralls.io', 'circleci.com', 'github.com/actions',

However, there are some strategies to get a better icon:\n\n1. **Use `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/{owner}/{repo}/HEAD/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png`** — Fastlane metadata often has the app icon\n2. **Check for common icon files in the repo root**: `icon.png`, `app_icon.png`, etc. via `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/{owner}/{repo}/HEAD/icon.png`\n3. **Use the GitHub Social Preview image**: `https://opengraph.githubassets.com/1/{owner}/{repo}` — this is the social media preview card, shows the repo image\n4. **Use the favicon/icon from the repo\'s homepage** — complex, requires fetching the website\n\nThe most reliable and commonly found approach for open source apps:\n- Try `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/{owner}/{repo}/HEAD/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png` (Android Fastlane)\n- Try `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/{owner}/{repo}/HEAD/icon.png`\n- Fallback to `owner.avatar_url` (current behavior)\n\nHowever, these raw.githubusercontent.com URLs might not always work and would require testing.\n\nA better approach that\'s commonly used:\n- **Use the GitHub opengraph image**: This is available at `https://opengraph.githubassets.com/1/{owner}/{repo}` but it\'s the social card, not an icon.\n\nActually, the most practical solution for an app store showing GitHub repos is to:\n1. LetterAvatar\n\nBut this would require fetching multiple URLs in sequence which is slow and not great UX.\n\nA better approach: In `AppIcon`, maintain an index of current URL attempt, try the next one on error. This is called a "cascading fallback" pattern.\n\nLet me implement this:\n- `AppIcon` receives `owner`, `repo`, `avatarUrl`, `name`, `size`\n- Internally maintains a list of URLs to try\n- Shows the first one that loads successfully\n- Falls back to LetterAvatar if all fail\n\nThe URL candidates in order:\n1. `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/{owner}/{repo}/HEAD/fastlane/metadata/android/en-US/images/icon.png` (common for Android apps)\n2. `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/{owner}/{repo}/HEAD/app_icon.png`\n3. `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/{owner}/{repo}/HEAD/icon.png`\n4. `{avatarUrl}` (owner avatar)\n\nFor performance, I won\'t add too many fallbacks — let\'s do 3 specific candidates + avatar fallback.\n\nChanges needed:\n1. `AppItem` type: add `owner` and `repo` fields (already there!) \n2. `AppIcon.tsx`: add cascading URL fallback logic\n3. `AppCard.tsx`: pass `owner` and `repo` to `AppIcon`\n4. `detail/[id].tsx`: pass `owner` and `repo` to `AppIcon`\n\nLet me update `AppIcon` to use the cascading approach and update callers.\n\nActually, looking at AppCard, it already passes `app.avatar_url` and `app.name`.
